Fourth Plenary Session

Today's Opening Ceremony

Preliminary Meeting Blocked

Auditorium Decoration Completed

(Nanjing) The Fourth Plenary Session is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 9:00 AM on the 20th. The Central General Affairs Section has completed the decoration of the auditorium. From the main gate to the auditorium, colorful paper flowers and red plaques with gold characters are hung. The horizontal plaque at the main gate reads: "The Chinese Kuomintang Central Executive Committee's Fourth Plenary Session." The couplet reads: "Develop the spirit of political tutelage, unite revolutionary forces." The horizontal plaque at the second gate reads: "Common Struggle." The couplet reads: "Unify will, contribute effectively." The horizontal plaque in the auditorium reads: "Sincere Unity." The couplet reads: "Pool wisdom, act on words." The opening ceremony includes: 1. Opening of the meeting; 2. Central Committee members take their seats; 3. Playing music; 4. Singing the Party song; 5. Bowing three times to the Party flag and the portrait of the Premier; 6. Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; 7. Silent tribute for three minutes; 8. Chairman delivers the opening address; 9. Playing music; 10. Photography; 11. Adjournment. (19th Dispatch)

Preliminary Meeting to be Held Immediately After the Opening

(Nanjing) The Fourth Plenary Session will hold a preliminary meeting immediately after the opening ceremony on the 20th. The 21st will be a day of rest. At 9:00 AM on the 22nd, an enlarged commemorative week will be held, with Dai Jitao attending to give a report. The official meeting will be held after the commemorative week. (19th Telegram)

Central Secretariat Busy with Preparations

(Nanjing) The Central Secretariat has completed all preparations for the opening of the plenary session on the morning of the 20th. The inside and outside of the Party headquarters and the grand auditorium are decorated with flowers and plaques, creating a new atmosphere. The order of the meeting has also been determined. On the 19th, more than a dozen Central Committee members from various places continued to arrive in Beijing. Important figures were constantly arriving at various train stations, docks, and hotels. The reception section of the Party headquarters was busy with receptions. The Publicity Committee also took live-action sound movies during the opening ceremony. The staff of the Central Secretariat will work as usual on Sunday, the 21st, which is a regular holiday. All routine meetings of the Central Government will be suspended during the plenary session. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Guangdong Case Will Be the Focus of Discussion

(Nanjing) A certain Central Committee member said that there are not many proposals from various parties regarding military, political, and diplomatic issues at this Fourth Plenary Session. Therefore, the most important case is the proposal submitted by the Central Committee members in the Southwest based on Hu Hanmin's eight-point proposal, which will be the focus of discussion. After Chairman Chiang arrives in Beijing, an informal meeting will be held first, and then the agenda will be discussed. (19th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to a certain committee member, the Guangdong Committee will come to Beijing within a few days. The Guangdong proposal was previously brought to Beijing by Sun Ke, but Sun only brought a letter of opinion without a formal proposal. The content focuses on rectifying Party discipline and revitalizing politics, and advocates that the military listen to the government and the government listen to the Party. The original text of this letter of opinion was revised by Chuan Bingchang and recorded by Wu Ti-yun, and is Wu's last work, a valuable historical document for the Party. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Central Committee Members from Various Places Arrive in Beijing One After Another

(Nanjing) Central Committee members Yu Youren, Zhang Zhiben, Huang Fusheng, Sun Jingya, Wang Boqun, Chu Minyi, Huang Shaoxiong, etc. arrived in Beijing by overnight train from Shanghai at 7:00 AM on the 19th to attend the plenary session. Yu said that he intends to propose a thorough exemption of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies and surcharges on land taxes to relieve the people's suffering, and will submit it to the plenary session after making slight adjustments. The proposals for this plenary session, in light of the painful lessons learned after the Fujian turmoil, will concentrate on rectifying Party affairs to consolidate the Party's foundation. Zhang said that he has no proposals for the plenary session. Most of the Shanghai committee members can attend. It is heard that the Shanghai committee has a proposal to discuss strengthening national defense, which will be submitted to the meeting. Huang Shaoxiong said that he did not go to the front to meet Chairman Chiang during his visit to Zhejiang, and there were no special tasks in Hangzhou. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Central Committee members Fang Juehui, Zhang Weicun, and Deng Jiayan also arrived in Beijing from Jinan at 8:30 AM on the 19th to attend the plenary session. Fang said that he has no proposals. During his visit to Qingdao, Jinan, and other places, he met with Shen Honglie and Han Fuqu. The political situation in Shandong Province is very safe. The remnants of Liu Guitang's bandit gang are currently scurrying near Handan and have not been able to cross the Yellow River after being attacked by a large army. They have not entered Shandong Province. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Shao Lizi arrived in Beijing by Eurasia No. 2 plane from Xi'an at 5:00 PM on the 19th. He said that he has no proposals for the plenary session, but he has already made suggestions to the Central Government and the Economic Committee on the construction and relief of the Northwest, and he still intends to present them to the plenary session at an appropriate time, and ask the committee members to jointly preside over it. The current situation in Shaanxi is peaceful, and all parties can proceed in an orderly manner, but the conflict between Sun and Ma is quite worrying. He and Yang Hucheng jointly telegraphed Sun Dianying on the morning of the 19th, advising him to stop his westward advance and wait for the Central Government to resolve it. Deng Baoshan arrived in Shaanxi yesterday and discussed with Yang Hucheng plans to maintain peace and security in the Northwest, and entrusted Yu to report to the Central Government. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Central Committee members Zhou Fo-hai and Yu Bing-tang arrived in Beijing by train from Zhenjiang at 2:30 PM on the 19th. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Hangzhou) Central Committee members Lu Diping, Chen Bulei, and Zeng Yangfu left Hangzhou together by express train with an attached sleeping car at 9:50 AM this morning to go to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. Provincial government affairs will be handled by Wang Cheng-ying, the acting provincial committee member. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen, Lu Diping, Wu Zhihui, and Wang Boqun arrived in Beijing from Shanghai at 9:30 PM on the 19th. Yu Bing-tang came from Zhenjiang in the same car. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Beiping) Shang Zhen will leave Beiping tomorrow morning to go to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. (19th Dispatch)

(Zhenjiang) Chen Guofu, Zhou Fohai, Wang Boling, Cheng Tianfang, and Yu Jingtang went to Beijing by private car on the 19th to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. (19th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to reliable sources, Zhang Xueliang did not depart on the evening of the 19th due to some matter and will change to coming to Beijing from Shanghai on the night of the 20th. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang is scheduled to arrive in Beijing on the morning of the 20th and has telegraphed friends in Beijing to book rooms at the Lizi Society to prepare for his stay. (19th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Song Ziwen got off the train at Koping Gate at 9:30 AM on the 19th and went to his private residence in Beijige. He plans to attend the plenary session tomorrow morning. It is heard that Song has no proposals this time. (19th Dispatch)

Zhangjia Sends Li Jianzhang to Attend

(Beiping) The Mongolian Banner Commissioner Zhangjia sent a telegram to Jianzhang, the resident Beijing secretary of the commissioner's office, on the 19th, asking him to represent him at the Fourth Plenary Session and informing the Secretariat of the Assembly. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Cheng Qian and Others Propose a National Salvation Plan

(Nanjing) It is widely rumored that Central Committee members Cheng Qian and others in Shanghai will submit a national salvation plan to the Fourth Plenary Session for discussion. It is heard that the main points are roughly to expand the powers of the Standing Committee of the Central Political Council to achieve the effect of centralized rule. As for the original members of the Standing Committee, Wang Zhaoming, Chiang Kai-shek, and Hu Hanmin, the three members have built a lot for the Party and the country and are highly respected at home and abroad, so it is still advocated that they be re-elected. The issue of the division of powers between the central government and the provinces is also planned to be raised for discussion, appropriately dividing the powers to adjust the chaos of the past. It is said that this case has been endorsed by most of the Shanghai committee members such as Zhang Renjie and Li Yuwin. (19th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Zhang Zhiben said that he has no special opinions on the conference. He only co-signed with Committee Member Cheng Qian in Shanghai on a national defense proposal, which has been directly sent to the Central Secretariat from Shanghai. Committee Member Li Liejun will propose two cases to the conference: opening up political power and reforming politics. Li is afraid that he will not be able to come to Beijing to attend the meeting due to illness. Sun Jingya said that the Shanghai Committee, led by Cheng Qian, jointly submitted a proposal to the plenary session to consolidate national defense and formally organize a National Defense Committee. He has already signed the proposal. (19th Dispatch)

Liu Zhi Plans to Have Two Proposals

(Nanjing) Liu Zhi arrived in Beijing from Bian on the morning of the 19th. He said that he has two proposals to the conference: one is to improve education so that poor children have the opportunity to study, and the other is the land issue to realize the equalization of land ownership and the tillers own their land. Banditry in Henan Province has been suppressed. The province has 371 security teams with excellent training results, which can protect the local area. Political affairs are realistic and gradually getting on track. Financial revenues and expenditures can also be matched, and education funds are completely independent. This year's administrative plan has been drafted, and there have been improvements in civil affairs, finance, education, and security. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Wang Ten Hosts a Banquet for Central Committee Members Arriving in Beijing

(Nanjing) Wang Shihe hosted a banquet at the official residence of the Ministry of Railways for Central Committee members Wang Faqin, Zhu Jiqing, Chen Yi, Zhang Qun, Shao Lizi, Tang Youren, Gu Mengyu, Wang Maogong, Chen Gongbo, and Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Headquarters, and more than a dozen others. (19th Dispatch)

Yizheng Salt Industry Groups Petition

(Nanjing) The Yizheng Twelve Fort Salt Industry Groups petitioned the Fourth Plenary Session, saying that it would be best if the salt administration authorities could delay the implementation of the new salt law to avoid shaking the foundation of the country. If the new law is to be strictly enforced, the Twelve Forts should still be the center of salt transportation in Huaihe. They listed ten benefits and asked not to listen to the salt transport envoy's proposal to move the Yangzhou Salt Company north. (19th Dispatch)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek

Arrived in Hangzhou Yesterday and Stayed at the Aviation School

Will Arrive in Beijing Today

(Hangzhou) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek took a Sikes aircraft and landed at Kuangqiao Airport at 3:40 PM on the 19th to refuel and then took the original plane to Beijing. Another message said that he stayed at the Aviation School on the evening of the 19th and is scheduled to fly to Beijing on the morning of the 20th. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Hangzhou) At 3:35 PM on the 19th, it was rumored here that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had flown to Kuangqiao. The Cheng Lu Executive Office sent many guards to cordon off the area to welcome him. Those who went to welcome him included Xu Peigen, Director of the Aviation Administration, Zhou Junyan, Director of the Finance Department, Lu Bichou, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, and Lu Dai, Secretary-General of the Provincial Government. The airport was heavily guarded. When the Ford aircraft arrived, it only carried Chiang's guards and luggage. According to those who welcomed him, the Ford aircraft will fly again on the morning of the 20th to welcome Chiang directly to Nanjing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session, or to stop in Hangzhou temporarily is yet to be determined. Deng Wenyi, Chiang's secretary, and four guards, who flew here on the 17th, said that it was a misunderstanding. (19th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek originally planned to fly to Beijing by plane on the morning of the 19th, but was unable to do so due to bad weather. According to a certain source, he changed to returning to Beijing on the 20th. All sectors of the capital's schools and institutions have scheduled to send representatives to Minggugong Airport to welcome him on the morning of the 20th. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Roosevelt's Far East Policy

Appears to be a Pacific Nanny

Maintaining the Stimson Non-Recognition Doctrine

Pu Yi's Usurpation to be Announced Tonight

(Washington) The Director of the Far Eastern Affairs Department of the State Department, Hornbeck, said in a speech today that the United States intends to import the international concept that Roosevelt used in South America and Central America into the Pacific and make all kinds of legal efforts to be a good neighbor in the Far East. He also said that the Stimson non-recognition of the situation created by force is still the policy of the United States. This is the first time that a responsible official of the Roosevelt administration has explained the United States' Far East policy. (18th Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) The Japanese-instigated Manchukuo Pu Yi's claim to the throne has attracted the attention of the authorities here. They have had discussions from time to time and feel that this matter is likely to cause a world war. Some people who pay attention to the Far East issue say that war cannot be avoided, or it will be after this spring, which is worrying. This kind of argument also appears in the newspapers and magazines here from time to time. The Japanese Embassy in Washington buys these books as soon as they see them, so they soon disappear from bookstores and are difficult to find. (18th National Telegram)

(Tokyo) An important announcement regarding Pu Yi's enthronement will be made at 5:00 PM tomorrow night. The spokesperson of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs declared today that Zheng Xiaoxu, the Prime Minister of Manchukuo, will issue an important declaration in Chinese, English, and Japanese at 5:00 PM tomorrow afternoon. The Tokyo Manchukuo Embassy will issue the same declaration one hour later, but only in Japanese. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Soviet Russia

Preparations for War Against Japan

Approximately Divided into Three Military Regions

(Beiping) According to reliable sources, the possibility of war between Japan and Russia is indeed urgent. The Japanese military is actively transporting to northern Manchuria. The Russian military has made proper military deployments. Preparations for war against Japan are divided into approximately three military regions: 1. The Coastal Province Military Region, based in Vladivostok; 2. The Amur Province Military Region, based in Khabarovsk; 3. The Transbaikal Province Military Region, based in Chita. Military Commissioner Vostretsov commands nine divisions and four brigades stationed in Khabarovsk, commanding the military affairs of the Coastal Province and Amur Military Regions. Bolhailov commands four divisions and three brigades stationed in Chita, commanding the military affairs of the Transbaikal Region. Powerful electrical networks, artillery fortresses, and wireless radio stations are installed outside Sanjiangkou. The distance between the fortresses is about 50 li, with an airport stationed in the middle with a squadron of aircraft. Fortresses are also built outside the sandbars outside Sanjiangkou and covered with electrical networks to control the border with Manchuria. The troops stationed in the lower reaches of the Heilongjiang River have been concentrated in Wushi on the opposite bank of Heihe, about 20,000. A large-scale airport with 28 squadrons of aircraft is located at Baojijialiu Station, 200 li northeast of Wushi, surrounding Manchuria. (19th Dispatch)

US Aggressive Shipbuilding Plan

Approved by the Budget Committee

Will be Submitted to Congress for Discussion Soon

(Washington) Former Senator Vincent's naval shipbuilding proposal has been approved by Thomas, Chairman of the Budget Committee, and will be submitted to Congress for discussion soon. Thomas claimed that Vincent's proposal does not conflict with the President's large naval plan. Vincent, as Chairman of the Senate Naval Affairs Committee, seeing the full expansion of the Japanese Navy and Britain having the same motive, strongly advocated shipbuilding as soon as possible. Senator Bilidon also had a similar proposal recently. The US government plans to build 101 battleships within four years from 1935, costing approximately 482 million US dollars. (18th National Telegram)

New British Dock Completed

The Largest in Scale in the World

(London) The new British Southampton George V dock, the largest dock in the world, was opened today. Lord Essendon, Chairman of the White Star Line Shipping Company, claimed that a new company will be organized to take over the assets of the Cunard and White Star shipping companies in the North Atlantic, but in all other respects, the two companies will maintain their separate status. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Italian Prime Minister's Anti-Japanese Remarks

Tokyo Lodges a Protest

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs received a telegram from Japanese Consul Fubi in Honolulu stating that on the 14th of this month, Honolulu newspapers reported that Rome telegraphed Italian Prime Minister Mussolini on the 13th to issue a Yellow Peril theory, especially attacking Japan's aggression. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that Italy has been induced by Soviet Russia and has recently shown anti-Japanese sentiments. Foreign Minister Hirota tonight ordered Japanese Ambassador to Italy Matsushima to lodge a protest with the Italian government. (19th China United Press Telegram)

French Scholars

Regret Our Loss of a Barrier

Pacific Problems Research Association

Attention to the Future of Our Country

(Paris) The Pacific Problems Research Association is organized by left-wing people, so Prime Minister Benawe and the current Minister of the Navy Salo are all initiators. The association met this morning. Mr. Berlioz (member of the French National Academy of Sciences, proficient in Chinese studies, who came to China last year) first spoke to pay tribute to the former Governor of Vietnam, Baskier. Unfortunately, Baskier died in a plane crash after returning to his country to give a lecture at the association. People regretted it. Later, Ai Sikala, Professor of Law at the University of Paris and consultant to the Chinese government, reported on his recent observations in China, saying that China has made important progress in material organization. Then, Father Robber, Elder of the Catholic Church of Trinity, and well-known journalist Le Rang held a debate. All those present said that the Chinese government has lost control over several provinces along the border, and it is regrettable that the barrier has been lost. (18th Havas Telegram)

Cao Haosen Arrives in Beijing

Will Go to the Military Department Immediately to Take Office

Yang Yongtai Came with Him

Gu Zhutong Will Succeed as Military Deputy

(Nanjing) Military Deputy Cao Haosen arrived in Beijing on the Jiangshun steamer from Hankou at noon on the 19th. Yang Yongtai, Secretary-General of the Executive Office, also came to Beijing with Cao on the same boat from Xunyang. More than 40 senior officials of the military department and Tang Youren, the Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, went to the wharf to welcome him. Cao said that he was ordered to return to Beijing to take charge of military affairs and went to the department to take office in the afternoon. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Chen Yi will go to Fujian to take office after meeting with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Beijing and asking for instructions. The trip is expected to be around the 23rd. The candidate for the successor of the military deputy has been internally determined to be Gu Zhutong, and the official order will be issued within a few days. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Cao Haosen returned to Beijing on the 19th and telegraphed He Yingqin to report his return to the department. He told reporters that the banditry in the three provinces of Hubei, Henan, and Anhui has been mostly suppressed. The mountainous areas of Lihuang County on the border of Henan and Anhui have been deeply affected by banditry, and there are still remnants of bandits who are being surrounded and suppressed by our army. The Sichuan bandits have been severely damaged by Liu Xiang's suppression. Heavy troops have been deployed on the border of Hubei, and the Sichuan bandits will be given a head-on blow if they flee east. Returning to Beijing to take charge of department affairs does not mean taking over. What was handled by Chen before will be handled by me, and Minister He will still be responsible to the outside world. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Central Army Crosses the River

Pursuing the 19th Route Army

A Major Battle is Imminent in Xinghua and Putian

Hai Chou Warship Transporting Troops to Xiamen

(Xiamen) A person from Fuzhou on the morning of the 18th said □□□□□·□□□ Regiment Li Liangrong entered □□□ Division one regiment first entered the city and disarmed a company of the 19th Route Army outside the city. Chiang Ting-wen and Zhang Zhen arrived in the afternoon. The Central Army took □□□ Division Li Regiment and the Eighth Division as the vanguard. On the 18th at dawn, they crossed the river south to pursue. They will take advantage of the 19th Route Army's retreat and deploy defenses to defeat them. The traffic between Zhangzhou and Quanzhou, and the ports of Shima and Anhai, is still difficult for travelers. (19th Dispatch) (Xiamen) The Central Army pursuit force is the Third and Ninth Divisions. They crossed the river from Xiadouwan Bianjiang on the morning of the 18th under the command of Wei Lihuang and will arrive in Xinghua on the 20th. A major battle will take place in Xinghua and Putian within one or two days. (19th Dispatch) (Xiamen) The Hai Chou warship arrived in Xiamen from the province on the morning of the 19th. It is heard that Zhang Zhizhong's regiment traveled with it. A regiment landed in Heshan, but it was very secretive and has not been verified. (19th Dispatch)

Trenches Widely Dug Outside Quanzhou

(Xiamen) A person from Quanzhou on the 17th said that trenches were widely dug outside the city and electrical networks were deployed. Only the South Gate is still open for traffic, and all others are closed. Zhangzhou is also heavily defended. Yang Regiment of Zhang Yan's army returned to Hehe and is stationed there with two regiments and two artillery battalions. (19th Dispatch)

Zhangzhou Political Security Division Established

(Xiamen) Xu Minghong established the Political Security Division in Zhangzhou and served as its division commander. He recruited from Longxi, Nanjing, Zhangpu, and Haicheng and has formed two regiments. Another regiment was formed from Zhangpu, Haicheng, and Nanjing, with the three county heads serving as battalion commanders. (19th Dispatch)

Speculation on the Future of the 19th Route Army

(Guangzhou) The future of the 19th Route Army is now being speculated on by people here. Whether Cai Tingkai's troops will withdraw to the Guangdong-Fujian border or to southern Fujian is still unknown. The 19th Route Army can only choose one of two paths: one is to retreat into Jiangxi Province and join the Communist army, and the other is to retreat to southern Fujian and surrender to Guangdong and be incorporated into Chen Jitang's army. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Current Affairs Commentary

A Word for the Fourth Plenary Session [By] Ting

The Northeast Incident. A rare and huge change in the modern history of the world. Such a blow. Not enough to awaken the government and the public of our country. Then the future of the entire Chinese nation. Will be hopeless. It's not just the loss of the country. At the time of the Fourth Plenary Session to discuss the great plan of [Consolidating the National Foundation and Revitalizing the Nation]. We dare to do our duty to the media. Briefly contribute our humble opinions.

(1) Before the Sino-Japanese War. The Japanese people deliberately planned to plot against Korea. Korea then perished. After that, they accumulated little by little to plot against Manchuria. The puppet organization became a reality. Now they want more. It will also involve North China. We should pay attention to observing the subtle details of the Japanese people's actions. Often seeing its intentions. For example, before the 918 Incident, the Japanese people wrote books. The discussion often mentions [Korea] and [Manchuria]. Now it is often referred to as [Korea], [Manchuria] and [North China]. For example, the cover illustrations of its national pictorials used to be mostly Manchurian monuments. Now it is replaced by famous places in North China. [When you step on frost, you know that thick ice is coming.] The origin is clear. I am afraid that North China's view of Manchuria. It will be like Manchuria's view of Korea. In recent days, it has been frequently reported that Puyi will soon claim the throne. Those who know say that the inside story of this matter. It's not the change of the [Manchukuo] Executive to the imperial system. But it is the plan of the [Qing Dynasty] to restore the abdicated emperor. The Japanese are taking the initiative from it. This is even more obvious to those with eyes. Like this conspiracy and ambition. Emerging endlessly. Future hidden worries. I don't know where it will end. Moreover, the international situation in the Far East. It is also becoming increasingly tense. Today, it is widely rumored that the crisis of 1936 is inevitable. Whether it is a Japanese-American war or a Japanese-Russian war. Our country cannot stand idly by. Just in terms of the current situation in our country today. May I ask how we can safely overcome this future difficulty.

(2) Rural bankruptcy. Industrial and commercial decline. People's livelihood is unstable. Banditry is frequent. All are serious problems today. Urgent need to solve. However, using military force to eliminate the superficial evil forces. It is only a palliative treatment. If you want to cure the root cause. The first is the improvement of politics. If the government is clean and bright. Then the people will live and work in peace and contentment. So as not to be forced into danger. Agriculture, industry and commerce. It can also be brought into line. Slowly develop. Last year, the customs import surplus reached a huge amount of 900 million yuan. Sufficient to be the gaze of the failure to reconcile production and consumption. The future of the national economy. How can we imagine. Those who plan for the country. Should know to prescribe the right medicine. Strive for the big ones.

(3) In today's national political system. Whether it is [Democracy] or dictatorship. Its governance is not outside the realm of a political group. If you want this group to exert its effectiveness. The three essential elements of doctrine, organization and cadre talent are indispensable. Today's main task of the Kuomintang. In strengthening its organization. Unite its cadre talent. Forming a whole powerful group. Only then can we implement its doctrine. Bear the responsibilities that should be fulfilled internally and externally. In addition, we should also recruit talents from outside the party. Collect public opinion widely. To overcome national difficulties together.

In short, the current national lifeline is full of holes and sores. All need to be remedied. It is really coming to the last moment. At the beginning of the opening of this Fourth Plenary Session. How should we discuss and cope with this [Extraordinary Time]'s actual approach. The people of the country are eagerly looking forward to it. Government leaders, make your last effort.

Legislative Yuan Meeting

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 45th meeting at 9:00 AM on the 19th. Wang Qi and 77 other people attended. Sun Ke presided over the meeting, with Liang Hancao as the Secretary-General. Matters discussed: (1) Review of the draft Postal Law. It was resolved to refer it to the Legal Committee to be reviewed jointly with the Economic Committee. (2) Review of the draft amendment to Article 6 of the Oath Regulations. It was resolved to refer it to the Legal Committee for review. (3) Committee members Jiao Yitang and Lou Tongsun reported on the review of the draft Cooperative Law. It was resolved to refer it to the original reviewing committee for review. (4) The Foreign Affairs Committee of this Yuan, together with the Labor Law Committee, reported on the review of the draft Convention on the Employment of Women Before and After Childbirth. It was resolved to pass it according to the review opinions and postpone ratification. (5) The Foreign Affairs Committee of this Yuan, together with the Labor Law Committee, reported on the review of the draft Convention on Night Work of Women. It was resolved to pass it according to the review report and postpone ratification. (6) The Foreign Affairs Committee of this Yuan, together with the Labor Law Committee, reported on the review of the draft Convention on Weekly Rest in Industrial Undertakings. It was resolved to approve it with reservations according to the review report. (7) The Foreign Affairs Committee of this Yuan, together with the Labor Law Committee, reported on the review of the draft Convention on Right of Association and Combination of Agricultural Workers. It was resolved to approve it according to the review report. (8) The Foreign Affairs Committee of this Yuan, together with the Labor Law Committee, reported on the review of the draft Convention concerning Equality of Treatment for National and Foreign Workers as regards Workmen’s Compensation for Accidents. It was resolved to approve it according to the review report. (19th Central News Agency Telegram)

Ma Telegraphed That Sun's Troops Were Pressing In

(Beiping) Ma Hongkui telegraphed to Ping this morning, saying that the majority of Sun Dianying's army had engaged in battle with my cavalry Ma Kui regiment at Shizuishan. Because we defended with natural barriers, Sun's army suffered heavy losses and is still in a stalemate. Its main force has been crossing the river from Wuyuan, Linhe, Dengkou, etc., since the 16th, intending to concentrate in Woye and attack the Hedong line, with the intention of breaking through Hengcheng and heading straight for the provincial capital. The advance party, led by the bandit Yang Monkey Kid, with more than 1,000 men, came into contact with the Second Cavalry Regiment in Taohutan and was dispersed. Coupled with the cold weather, most of them froze to death. Now, our Hedong line is very solid, and the enemy will never be able to advance further. As for the northern route, Sun used about two brigades of infantry and three regiments of cavalry to advance from Heguazi towards the Beizi area of A Banner. Because the area is sparsely populated and the entrances have been filled by the populace for a long time, and there is no food, coupled with the cold weather, which has reached minus six degrees, people and horses are dying. This time, Sun's army is advancing step by step, and central government orders are difficult to stop. Our army has a duty to defend the territory and cannot but make proper defenses. We have prepared the forces of the three provinces to respond in battle, waiting for the central government's order to launch a punitive expedition, which will not be difficult to annihilate. (Special telegram on the 19th)

Wang Shiping and He Yingqin Request Instructions

(Beiping) Sun Dianying sent a telegram to Chairman He of the Beiping Military Council: He Jun, I, Kuiyuan, am a martial man who has never studied. I am unworthy of being entrusted with military duties and serving the country with utmost sincerity. In the past, when Liaodong fell, the entire army gnashed its teeth. When the Battle of Rehe broke out, I was ordered to rush to aid. As the vanguard arrived in Chengde, enemy cavalry was already approaching Chifeng. I advanced hastily and encountered the enemy. Fortunately, the soldiers fought bravely and were able to avoid being annihilated despite being a lone army. When the battle situation stabilized, I was ordered to transfer defenses, without participating in the civil war. I repeatedly declared that the central government had thought deeply and planned for all sides, remembering that the Northeast had been lost and the Northwest was in danger. I was ordered to engage in reclamation and garrison the border in Qinghai, to control Xinjiang in the west and support Tibet in the south. The population is sparse, and wasteland awaits reclamation. The geography is important, and production is essential. It is my duty to serve the country, and I dare not refuse. Therefore, I led tens of thousands of hungry soldiers, not afraid of thousands of miles of expedition. Unexpectedly, as soon as I arrived in Ningxia, I received a telegram from Chairman Ma of Ningxia, refusing entry, claiming that he had received an order from Zhu Shaoliang, director of the Gansu-Shaanxi Pacification Headquarters, that the 41st Army was not allowed to set up supply stations or pass through Gansu, Ningxia, and Qinghai. I then received a telegram from Chairman Ma, stating that the vanguard of your army should immediately retreat to the vicinity of the Wula River and not advance any further, and that Qinghai troops had been sent to the central part of the area and a part of Hu Zongnan's troops had been sent to Haiyuan. Director Zhu would arrive in Ningxia in the near future. I then received a telegram from Chairman Ma, saying that since the central government issued the order for your army to reclaim and garrison Qinghai, it had not notified Ningxia. Now, Director Zhu has strictly ordered that your army not advance westward. The facts are there and can be verified. At that time, in order to avoid conflict, I ordered the troops to stop advancing. For several months, they have been stranded in the wasteland, suffering all kinds of hardships. The barracks are not enough, so they dig earth kilns. In the desolate area, the soldiers are poorly clothed and fed. The miserable situation is unbearable to describe. The primary desire of people is to survive. It is unheard of to die in the wilderness. Therefore, I consulted with the Shanxi-Suiyuan authorities to temporarily allocate the wasteland of Wolin for reclamation. The troops were sent to the Woye, but they still did not cross the west of Suiyuan, but due to geographical limitations, they passed through a corner of Ningxia. Ningxia again sent a large army to intercept them. All the details have been reported by telegram. Later, I received your telegram and immediately ordered the troops to stop going to Woye. I did not expect that Chairman Ma would fabricate reasons and report to you, falsely accusing my troops of invading Ningxia in order to distort the truth. Recently, I received a telegram from Ping stating that you had mistakenly believed the Ningxia report and stopped issuing supplies to my troops. I cannot help but sigh upon hearing the news. I believe that my troops have obeyed the central government and have not dared to deviate in the slightest. Although they have endured extreme hardships, they have no complaints. If you lightly listen to one side's words and stop all the supplies, then tens of thousands of officers and soldiers will not die under the anti-Japanese swords, but will die from hunger and cold. If this is the case, what more can be said? I am grateful for your care for your subordinates. At this time, I beg you to carefully examine the facts and clearly discern right from wrong. Then, the officers and soldiers of my troops will have no regrets even if they starve to death. I present this to you with utmost urgency. Sincerely, Sun Kuiyuan. (Special telegram on the 19th)

Sun Telegram Claims to Have Obeyed Orders to Stop Advancing

(Nanjing) Sun Dianying's office in Nanjing stated on the 17th that my army began to negotiate with Director Yan to temporarily station in Woye in order to alleviate difficulties. The Ningxia side suddenly intercepted them, and it is not known what the intention was. I reluctantly fought back for self-defense, but in order to avoid escalating the matter, I have obeyed the order to stop advancing and await the central government's resolution. I hope that the central government will send a senior official to the front to monitor the Ningxia side to stop military actions and monitor my army to go to Woye to clarify the truth. (Special telegram on the 19th)

Regarding the issue of returning to Tibet, he will be able to decide after asking the central government for instructions. After returning to the north, he plans to go to Qinghai first to organize the Xuanhua Commissioner's Office and promote the central government's goodwill in order to promote the unity of the Mongolian and Han nationalities and save the country from disaster. Qin Dechun Visits Chaisan

Negotiating the Chahar East Incident

Questioning the Japanese and Puppet Troops' Intrusion into Zhaojiatun

The Japanese Side Claims It Was Due to a Misunderstanding in Suppressing Bandits

Japanese Troops in Zhaojiatun Withdraw to Heihe

(Beiping) Heihe News: The Japanese and puppet troops attacked Zhaojiatun, Longmensuo, on the 16th. Because Zhang Renjie and other three divisions were calm and prepared, they firmly defended their positions. Knowing that there were preparations, the Japanese and puppet troops retreated to Heihe. Song, because this kind of disturbance by the Japanese and puppet troops could affect the security of Chahar Province, specially telegraphed Qin Dechun to negotiate with the Japanese side. Qin visited Military Attaché Chaisan at the Japanese Embassy this afternoon and declared to Chaisan that Longmensuo and Zhaojiatun are both west of the Great Wall line, and Longmensuo is 15 miles from the Great Wall. The Japanese and puppet troops' intrusion into Zhaojiatun this time is clearly an action that has crossed the Great Wall line. He hopes that the Japanese side will find a way to stop it. Chaisan replied that he was not in Ping when this incident occurred. He sent a telegram to Chengde to ask Military Attaché Genben. He has now received a reply from Nishiyiyi, the commander of the 8th Division, stating that it was a misunderstanding caused by the suppression of bandits. Now, the Japanese troops in that area have withdrawn to the east of Heihe. The original defending Japanese troops will never advance west of the Great Wall. He hopes to convey this intention to Song Zheyuan. Qin immediately reported the situation of his meeting with Chaisan to Song in Tianjin. A telegram from Zhangjiakou reported that the situation in eastern Chahar was very peaceful. (Special telegram on the 19th)

(Beiping) There is no activity from the Japanese and puppet troops in eastern Chahar. The Jiaoji Railway Council

Discusses the Redemption of the Railway

(Nanjing) The Jiaoji Railway Council held a meeting on the 19th, attended by Wang Zhengting, Ge Guangting, Sa Fujun, Yan Deqing, etc. Wang Zhengting chaired the discussion on the redemption of the railway, and all agreed that it is imperative to raise funds as soon as possible to redeem the railway while the Japanese currency is plummeting. (Central News Agency telegram on the 19th)

(Nanjing) The Jiaoji Railway Council held a meeting on the 19th, attended by Chairman Wang Zhengting and directors Yan Deqing, Cui Shijie, Ge Guangting, Su Shenghai, etc. Ge said: 1. The points to be discussed by this council are the reorganization and development of railway affairs and transportation issues. 2. The Jiaoji Railway was built by Germany and occupied by Japan. When our country took over Qingdao, it paid a price of 40 million to recover the railway from Japan. The repayment of the loan has not yet been repaid. It is necessary to repay interest of 2.4 million per year. The operating income is about 1.6 million per month. After deducting all expenses of about 1.2 to 1.3 million per month and allocating the debt interest due to the Japanese side on schedule, there is little left. The average annual surplus is at most only about 3 million. In the future, it is necessary to start by developing business. In terms of operating income, freight accounts for the majority, averaging 75% per month. Passenger transport accounts for a small number. (Special telegram on the 19th)

The Sheng'an Steamer Robbery Case

Involves Many Foreigners

(Dalian) The number of people involved in the Sheng'an Steamer robbery case on June 28th last year is increasing. Matsumoto, the defense lawyer appointed by the Japanese court, recently requested the authorities to summon a German from Shanghai, two Germans, a Japanese from Tokyo, and two Chinese from Tianjin who had previously served as aviators, and a German who had served as an aviator, to testify here so that they could be questioned during the retrial on the 15th of next month. He also requested to summon a British man from the shipping industry, a Lithuanian man from the hotel industry, and a White Russian officer. Although the number of witnesses is not yet known, the involvement of so many foreigners in the case has attracted the attention of people here. The authorities attach great importance to this case. It is expected that the court's decision will not only have a significant impact on Japanese criminal law and maritime law, but also on the part of international law relating to maritime piracy. The chief justice in charge of the case told a Reuters reporter that the reason why the case was delayed until the retrial on February 15th was to facilitate the consideration and decision by the Dalian District Court authorities on the following two points: (1) Does the Japanese authorities have the right to try the five European nationals who are the main culprits in this case? (2) Has the defendant violated Japanese law? If the Japanese authorities do not have the right to try the foreign defendants, the court is prepared to dismiss the case and hand over the offenders to their respective consular officials for trial. If the court believes that it has the right to try the case, it is prepared to conclude the case within two or three weeks. According to Japanese law, if the offenders in this case are found guilty, they will be sentenced to death. If they are sentenced to imprisonment, they will be sent to the Lushunkou prison for detention. Matsumoto, the defense lawyer for the offenders, said that he is waiting for an opportunity to dismiss the case. He will base his defense on the following points: (1) The Japanese authorities have no right to try foreigners who kill foreigners on foreign ships outside Japanese territory. (2) The criminal conduct of the five victims is entirely piracy, and there is no Japanese law that can be cited as the basis for a verdict. (3) The German authorities are eager to extradite the German in the case for trial by the German court. (4) No matter how fair the Japanese court's decision is, the result will inevitably cause unfavorable repercussions. (Reuters telegram on the 17th)

Jiang Kanghu Regains Freedom

(Nanjing) Jiang Kanghu regained his freedom before dawn on the 19th. Jiang said that he would not leave Beijing for the time being so that all parties could understand that he had no political activities. (Special telegram on the 19th)

The Huayin Arsenal Has Been Shut Down

(Nanjing) The Huayin Arsenal, which is directly under the Ministry of Military Administration, has been poorly managed internally and is also experiencing financial difficulties. Huai River Guidance Committee

Mandatory Registration for Huai River Tenants

(Nanjing) The Huai River Commission recently issued a notice setting a three-month deadline for tenants in the Huai River basin of Jiangsu Province to register their leases. The registration period is from January 15th to February 15th, and registration is free. The fee will be five cents in the second month and ten cents in the third month. Leases will be revoked if they are not registered by the deadline. Administrative and judicial organs will be notified that any leases not presented for registration will be considered invalid. (Central News Agency dispatch, 19th)

Liu Zhi to be in Nanjing

To Discuss Temporary Measures for Yellow River Control

(Nanjing) Liu Zhi stated that in addition to attending the plenary session in Nanjing this time, he also plans to discuss temporary measures for Yellow River control with Chairman Chiang, President Wang, Standing Committee Member Song, the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission, and the Huai River Commission. After the Yellow River flood last year, not only Henan Province suffered severely, but Hebei and Shandong Provinces also suffered deeply. However, the dike project in Henan Province is slightly better than those in other provinces. However, the flood from the breach in neighboring provinces spread to Henan Province, making it impossible to prevent. Therefore, the first step in preventing future disasters should be simultaneous action by all provinces for easier results. The cost of temporary measures is estimated to be over ten million. Three methods are proposed for the central government to choose from: (1) Issue public bonds for Yellow River control, with the central and local governments sharing the responsibility for repayment in the future. (2) Allocate American wheat loans. (3) Railway surcharges. If any of these three can be chosen and implemented, there will be considerable results. In Henan Province, there are still more than 300,000 disaster-stricken refugees, and the provincial government is funding their resettlement along the Pinghan Railway. (Special dispatch, 19th)

England, America and France Agree on Stabilizing Exchange Rates

British and American Exchange Rate at Five US Dollars

French Exchange Rate at Seventy Seven Francs

(New York) The Commercial Daily reported today that the United States and Britain have agreed to maintain the stability of the exchange rate between the pound and the dollar temporarily at a ratio of five to one. The American Equalization Fund will protect the pound, and the British Equalization Fund will maintain the exchange rate of one pound at approximately seventy-nine francs. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

(London) Reliable sources from leading financial circles in London stated that the US government has reached an agreement with the central banks of Britain and France to stabilize the exchange rates between the three countries, Britain, France, and the United States, and that they have agreed that the exchange rate between Britain and the United States will be five US dollars and the exchange rate between Britain and France will be seventy-seven francs. American banks here, representing the US Federal Reserve Board, are purchasing gold here at the newly set price. This move is actually enough to prevent the US dollar from rising further. (National Telegram, 18th)

(London) The New York Commercial Daily carried a report that the pound and the dollar would be stabilized at a ratio of five to one, but insiders here do not easily believe it. Today, the US dollar has shown a reactionary trend in the London market, as the public believes that the current upward trend is only the result of general disappointment because the United States has not established a free gold market. It is expected that the US dollar will continue to rise temporarily, because the inflow of US funds has only just begun. The purchase of US bonds by Continental Europe shows that confidence in the stability of the US dollar is gradually recovering. American bankers estimate that US funds deposited in London are 100 billion yuan, and Canadian funds deposited in London are 50 billion yuan. Some sources say that the large-scale sale of francs was done by a certain legal bank in London, which is a sign that the French authorities are trying to prevent the franc from continuing to rise. Others say that the sale of francs was due to funds being transferred from Paris to London via London. However, well-informed sources say that the purchase of pounds in Paris this morning was because a certain party in France believed that, regardless of the US dollar, the current price of the pound was too low. (Reuters dispatch, 19th)

US House Currency Committee Passes

Gold Yuan Devaluation Plan

US Abandonment of Gold Standard Forced by Britain

Equalization Fund to Prevent Being Threatened Again

(Washington) The House Currency Committee discussed President Roosevelt's dollar devaluation plan and passed it by a vote of fifteen to one. The committee prepared a report on the president's plan, saying that the United States' abandonment of the gold standard was forced by Britain. The government suggested using 200 billion yuan as a fund to stabilize exchange rates, the purpose of which is to prevent this situation from happening again. It also said that the United States has the right to self-defense, and that when the interests of the American people are threatened by other countries' low-priced currencies, the United States also has the right to protect them. This layer should be recognized by the public. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

(Washington) The House of Representatives will deliberate on the dollar devaluation case on Saturday and Sunday. It is estimated that the case can be sent to the Senate in the middle of next week. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has asked Congress to pass it as soon as possible. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

(Washington) The Senate Banking Committee today amended President Roosevelt's request to authorize the Treasury Department to issue interest-free bonds. Committee Chairman Fletcher proposed this amendment, increasing the amount of bonds that the Treasury Department can issue by 25 billion yuan. Fletcher's move was on behalf of the Treasury Department, and Treasury Department officials said that this amendment allows the government to redeem any government bonds already issued with new bonds, thus making it easier for the Treasury Department to handle large-scale bond exchange businesses. As for whether this amendment allows the issuance of interest-free bonds in small denominations, it was not explained. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

New York Exchange Market

Gold Pounds and US Dollars Compete

(New York) The characteristic of today's foreign exchange market is the competition between the pound and the dollar. As a result, the pound closed at four dollars and ninety-six cents, lower than yesterday's seven cents. The highest value of the US dollar was stipulated to be quite low at sixty percent. Britain and France are afraid of adopting self-defense plans. This is the reason for the decline in the pound exchange rate. American funds have slightly flowed back overseas, and foreigners have invested in US securities again. This is another reason for the high price of the US dollar today. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

European War Panic

French Doubts About Germany

Cannot Disarm Without Agreement

Senate Votes Confidence in Government

(Paris) The Senate debated foreign affairs today and discussed the possibility of war, but not in the Pacific, but in Europe itself. Prime Minister Chautemps said that while countries are rearming, France cannot reduce its army and reduce its armaments. It can only be implemented after a future agreement is concluded. Several speakers expressed their belief that if Germany invades in the future, Britain will come to France's aid as in 1914. After Chautemps declared that the French army would never be reduced, the Senate passed a vote of confidence in the government by a large majority, with 257 votes in favor and only three votes against. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

(Paris) The Senate's discussion of the question on foreign affairs has ended. Foreign Affairs Committee Chairman Bérenger proposed a motion advocating faithful adherence to the League of Nations covenant and the Locarno Treaty, and trusting the government to engage in peaceful construction within the scope of the League of Nations, so that France's relations with various countries tend to be friendly, and to consolidate national defense and security. This motion was passed by a majority of 257 votes to three.

Do Not Go Too Far Against the German Nation

Before the vote, Prime Minister Chautemps restated the main points of Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour's speech, stating that France has always attached importance to the sovereignty of all nations and will never interfere in Germany's internal affairs. Chautemps continued, saying that the Germans fabricated rumors to slander France in order to arouse the German people's national ideology. This must have a dangerous impact on the country's foreign policy. It should be known that since the end of the European War, France has made concessions to Germany again and again. France's intention is nothing more than to express its hope for peace, and it believes that Germany has the right to restore its status as a great power, so it does not go too far against the German nation to make it difficult for them to endure. Unexpectedly, Germany did not understand that when the Geneva Disarmament Conference was about to reach a unanimously agreed solution, Germany suddenly withdrew from the conference. Can such an action not cause suspicion?

France's Security Has Only Two Paths

France believes that there are only two ways to ensure national security. If it does not rely on its own strength, it must rely on international cooperation. This view is very reasonable and should not be regarded as a contradiction. What we call disarmament means that we will implement disarmament in accordance with the methods stipulated in the general disarmament convention after the convention is established, and not that France should reduce its armaments at present, because there are still other countries that are rearming.

British-French Compromise is the Cornerstone of Peace

Chautemps continued, saying that France has always maintained its close compromise with various countries. For other major countries that do not have a close compromise with France but are the main factors for France's security, they also promote friendly relations, such as Britain. Our compromise with Britain is becoming increasingly consolidated, and it is a cornerstone of world peace. From this point of view, international cooperation is of great benefit to national defense policy.

Always Faithfully Adhere to the League of Nations Covenant

When Chautemps spoke about the League of Nations issue, he said that France has always faithfully adhered to the League of Nations Covenant. Even if the Covenant is amended, it should also be conditional on international cooperation, and a main body organization should not be formed separately by major countries within the League of Nations. As for direct negotiations on disarmament issues, they are based on the final result of the last adjournment of the Disarmament Conference, and should not deviate from the scope of the League of Nations Covenant. Therefore, although individual negotiations can be conducted by various countries at present, the Disarmament Conference should still be the final destination. In the end, all countries can conduct negotiations, but in any case, they cannot aim at rearming. World peace should be based on mutual trust among all nations, and the temporary balance of power and general psychological terror among nations should not be relied upon as the foundation of peace. Chautemps concluded by requesting Congress to grant him the necessary powers to carry out the policies he announced. All the congressmen applauded him enthusiastically. Lémery, one of the most important congressmen who raised the question, declared after the prime minister's speech that Prime Minister Chautemps had allowed for no reduction in France's military strength. At this point, the motion of confidence in the government proposed by Bérenger was put to a vote, with 257 votes in favor and three votes against. The government won. (Havas dispatch, 18th)

League of Nations Resolution

Guarantee Danzig Constitution

National Socialist Behavior

No Further Investigation for the Time Being

(Geneva) One of the important items on the agenda of today's League of Nations Council meeting was the constitution of the Free City of Danzig, as the League of Nations is the guarantor of the constitution of the Free City of Danzig. Recently, since the National Socialist Party in Danzig intends to gain power, several newspapers have been ordered to cease publication. League of Nations Commissioner Rusting (Danish) has reported this matter to the League of Nations. However, at today's Council meeting, the permanent inspector of the Danzig incident, also the British councilor in the Council, stood up and declared that the effectiveness of the current constitution has not been hindered in any way, and that the banned newspapers have now been republished, so the League of Nations does not need to investigate this matter further. The inspector also advocated that the Council should solemnly announce the meaning of the League of Nations' guarantee of the Danzig constitution again, that is, the progress of Danzig's public life should be based on the scope of the constitution, and the League of Nations is paying attention to this. Later, Dr. Rauschning, Chairman of the Danzig Free City Senate, reiterated that the current government of Danzig is determined to abide by the current constitution and will not dare to change it, and thanked the British inspector for the correctness of his statement. After Mr. Lau's speech, British Foreign Secretary Simon and French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour both spoke one after another, pointing out that the Danzig constitution has clearly stated the freedom of speech, and although the League of Nations is unwilling to exercise its power at this time, it still reserves its right to inquire whether the Danzig government is sincerely fulfilling its constitution. Simon's report was accepted by the Council. (National Telegram, 28th)

Illicit Road Purchase Negotiations Encounter Setbacks

(Tokyo) The Russian Ambassador to Japan, Yurelev, visited Foreign Minister Hirota yesterday afternoon to discuss the problems of lowering fares on the East Railway, the abolition of gold rubles, and the burgeoning movement against the use of counterfeit currency. Therefore, he hoped that Japan would intervene to seek a satisfactory solution. The Foreign Minister replied that this was an internal problem of the East Railway and should be resolved through local negotiations. Next, the Russian Ambassador stated that if the [Manchukuo] authorities release the Soviet personnel currently arrested in [Manchukuo], he requested mediation so that [Manchukuo] would understand that the successors to these personnel would be arbitrarily selected by the Director of the Road Bureau. The Foreign Minister again replied that he would wait for the local negotiations. The meeting ended at 6:30 PM. (19th Electric News)

According to another report, when Mori Island Consul-General stationed in Harbin and Komatsubara, the chief of the Harbin Special Service Agency, met with Russian Consul-General Slavitsky on the 14th, Consul-General Slavitsky Feng Sen opened and put forward the condition that although [Manchukuo] released the Russian personnel, unless the authority to appoint their successors was entrusted to the Director of the Administration Bureau, it would be difficult to reopen negotiations on the China Eastern Railway. In recent days, in addition to preparing everything, Changchun has been building an ascension altar for the puppet Puyi to ascend the throne on March 1st. The altar is six levels high and one hundred meters in diameter, a truly unprecedented and strange phenomenon. The Japanese and puppet forces plan that after Puyi ascends the throne, they will first invade Chahar and then develop into Guan Nei. North China may be troubled from then on.

Amidst the voices of Puyi's ascendancy to the throne, the Japanese army in eastern Chahar has once again taken military action. The Japanese army is determined to seize Chahar as a preparation for defending against Russia. However, before the ferocious face is revealed, it will first adopt a policy of gradual encroachment, gradually invading westward. This morning, more than 200 Japanese troops from the Heihe area of eastern Chahar, together with about 700-800 men from Zhang HaiPeng's puppet army, carrying small steel cannons, machine guns, and armored vehicles, suddenly attacked Longmensuo east of Chicheng from Xifengkou and occupied the Zhao Jiaying and Wagou areas more than ten miles east of Longmensuo, attempting to attack Longmensuo. At the same time, two Japanese aircraft flew to the Longmensuo Chicheng area at approximately 11:00 AM today to scout our military movements. The garrison in Longmensuo, our side, is the Provisional Third Division's Song Tielin Brigade. He and Huang first sent personnel to negotiate with the Japanese side and will take action after clarifying the Japanese army's intentions. Tonight, Qin reported everything to Song by telephone. Song thought that the situation in eastern Chahar was critical and will come to Ping from Tianjin immediately to consult with the authorities on countermeasures.

The Japanese army's invasion of Chahar has been a predetermined plan. Although our side has seen through its conspiracy, it feels difficult in terms of both material resources and military strength. In addition to using diplomatic methods, there is no substantial preparation. The future is very dangerous. (Dated January 16th)

Sun's Troops March West, Leading to Disputes

Sun and Ma's Troops Have Been Locked in a Stand-Off at Shizuizi for Days

The Authorities Are Paying Extraordinary Attention and Have Sent Personnel to Seek Yan's Opinion

Beiping Correspondence: Since the Anti-Japanese War, Sun Dianying's troops were first stationed in Chahar territory. During the era when Feng Yuxiang organized the Allied Army in Chahar, Sun himself, in order to avoid being drawn into the vortex, requested to enter Qinghai to reclaim wasteland. When the Chahar situation became complex, the authorities did not want this army to march west in order to reduce disputes. The authorities issued an order appointing Sun Dianying as the Reclamation Commissioner for the Qinghai Border Region. Afterwards, after the resolution of the Chahar situation, the military and political authorities in Ningxia and Qinghai telegraphed one after another to prevent Sun's troops from entering the territory. Therefore, Sun's westward march became a problem. At that time, in order to avoid other complications, the authorities made several attempts to appease the situation before finally ordering Sun's troops to temporarily postpone the westward march and spend the winter in the Baotou Linhe area before making a decision. This kind of arrangement was originally an expedient measure and not a fundamental solution. The authorities in Ningxia and Qinghai provinces could rest assured for the time being, while Sun's troops were not satisfied with their demands and were somewhat resentful. As a result, things changed over time.

Sun's troops were originally organized into an army, and the number of people has always exceeded the quota. During the Anti-Japanese War, they vigorously expanded and were reorganized into the Ninth Army Corps, with three more armies under its command. After the end of the war, the authorities ordered a reduction, still reorganizing it into one army, but Sun not only did not reduce it, but instead increased it, totaling about 60,000 people. However, due to the financial difficulties in North China, the authorities only paid the salary of one army, allocating 250,000 yuan per month. Sun's troops, with a total of 60,000 men, were restricted by the salary, and they were unhappy and always sought a way out to achieve their great desires. Since being ordered to stop the westward march, they have been waiting for an opportunity to move in western Sui, while still actively preparing for the westward march, and also asking Jin Yan for assistance. Yan has adhered to the Monroe Doctrine in recent years, aiming to transfer guest troops and reorganize the interior. He often considered the lingering of 60,000-70,000 hungry troops in western Sui a disaster. Yan was very willing to see Sun's troops attempting to march west. This time, Sun's troops launched an advance, hampered by the Central Government's orders, using the excuse that the weather in western Sui was cold and freezing, making it impossible to station troops there, and they needed to divide up the fertile fields to avoid the wind and snow. They had obtained Yan's consent beforehand, and Yan had helped Sun with 200,000 yuan. After Sun's westward march plan was finalized, they marched west on the 13th of this month and occupied Dengkou County on the Ningbian border of western Sui, and gradually advanced towards the Shizuizi area. The Ningxia authorities, Ma Hongkui, had long been prepared to prevent Sun's troops from advancing. A cavalry company was stationed in the Dengkou area as a warning force, and the main force was stationed in the Shizuizi area, because Shizuizi was the gateway to Ningxia, a strategic location that could be defended. In recent days, Sun's troops have arrived near Shizuizi and have formally made contact with Ma's troops. The two sides are currently in a stand-off.

After the conflict between Sun and Ma's troops occurred, it attracted much attention. Sun and Ma themselves also telegraphed each other to report the situation. The Ping authorities telegraphed the Central Government to request instructions, and at the same time, they telegraphed Sun and Ma to stop military action. At the same time, because Yan Xishan carried significant weight in the northwest, Hou Cheng, the Chief of Staff of the Military Branch, was specially sent to Bin to seek Yan's opinion. Mr. Hou left Ping by car this morning (16th) with a personal letter from He Yingqin to Yan. In addition to seeking Yan's opinion, the letter also asked Yan to persuade Sun to order his troops to temporarily stabilize and not advance west.

Judging from the current situation, it is very difficult to stop Sun's troops from marching west, and a conflict between Sun and Ma's troops is inevitable. Because during this period of national crisis, the Min war has not yet ended, and the northwest is once again engaging in fratricidal warfare, causing much worry for the future of the country. We must find a way to resolve the disputes to avoid escalating the situation.

This morning, because of the conflict between Sun and Ma's troops, in order to understand the authorities' attitude and the truth of the situation, the reporter went to Juren Hall to visit He and inquire about everything. He was busy with official duties and was unable to meet, so he replied in writing with three points: (1) Before the truth of the conflict between Sun and Ma's troops is clarified, it is inconvenient to announce the handling methods. (2) The situation of the conflict between the two armies is as reported in the newspaper. (4) I will not attend the Fourth Plenary Session in Beijing. (Dated January 16th)

Suzhou

Seven Deserters Shot Dead on the Spot During a Search

The Third Regiment of the Supplementary Brigade of the Second Division of the Army stationed in Suzhou, Xu Tingyao's army, Huang Jie's troops, has strict discipline and is praised by the people of Suzhou. On the 17th, thirteen soldiers from the regiment's mortar company suddenly deserted, taking fifteen guns with them. The regimental headquarters immediately notified the Shuiyi'an Second District to order all teams to pay attention to the whereabouts of these deserters and report them at any time. At 7:00 PM on the 18th, these deserters were suddenly discovered near the Xiangshankou on the shore of Taihu Lake, about one mile away from Mudu Xukou. They forgot to bring the temple, and they were preparing to spend the night in the temple. Wang Rongyi, the captain of the first squad of the Fifth Water Police Team stationed there, reported to the Water Public Security District by telephone, which was then reported to the regimental headquarters. Jiang, the regimental adjunct of the regiment, led the company commanders of Lou and Qi and three platoons of soldiers and four machine guns to depart from Suzhou on foot. They arrived at Xukou at 1:00 AM on the 19th and joined forces with the local water and land police security regiment to surround the Renqiao, Xingqiao, Xiangshan Zui, and Xukou Xijiang areas on all four sides. The two sides confronted each other until dawn at 6:00 AM, when the deserters opened fire in a desperate struggle. The soldiers immediately retaliated and opened fire for about two hours, killing seven deserters. Five were captured, and another was found in a reed nest, but only six guns were recovered, with nine still missing. The captured deserters were all taken to Suzhou and interrogated by the regimental headquarters.

Horrific Murder of a Woman: The Murderer Zhang Wu Arrested

The strongman Zhang Wu, a 33-year-old from Funing, was currently performing at the Xujiang Grand Theater outside the city and living in a small house south of the Dayang Bridge. Three or four months ago, he became intimate with Shen Sushi, a young woman from Zhenze, Wujiang, and they began living together. Although Sushi's mother, Shen Wu, also lived in Zhang Wu's house, she was occasionally dissatisfied with Zhang's behavior towards her daughter. On the night of the heavy snow, Zhang Wu actually beat Shen Wu to death. He carried the body to the area behind the new building of the Hongsheng Match Company, a cluster of coffins in a public cemetery, dug a hole, and buried it. The matter was extremely secretive, with snowflakes covering the soil and a coffin placed on top. However, yesterday (the 19th) morning, the incident was discovered by Guo Qilong and Ni Rong, patrol officers from the Third Sub-precinct, who reported it to the officer Chen Rongzhou. The officer dispatched police to investigate and confirm the facts. Zhang Wu, Shen Sushi, and neighbors Li Guangsheng and Lu Decai were taken to the precinct for questioning. According to Shen Subei's confession, she was 20 years old and had planned to sell herself for money, but her mother found her in Shanghai and brought her back to Suzhou. That night, Zhang Wu first slapped her mother and then severely beat her lower body, even stomping on her mother's abdomen. Shortly after, she died. Afterwards, Zhang tied both her hands and feet to a long bench until he went to sleep and untied them. She wanted to report it, but fearing she would be killed, she endured and waited for an opportunity to appeal. Lu and others claimed they did not know the details. They were all handed over to the Third Sub-bureau. Meanwhile, personnel from the local court arrived to conduct an inspection. When the other coffin covering the burial site was removed, a body was clearly visible in the snowy mud, with its upper body still exposed outside the soil.

Theft Suspect Escapes from Detention Center

Sun Hao, alias Di Sheng, a 28-year-old from Nantai, Tenth District, Wu Yi, was a theft suspect awaiting trial at the Wu Yi Detention Center. Wuxi

Ship Sinks, Drowning Two

Xu Huilin, a man from Yancheng, Jiangbei, in his thirties, made a living by steering a stone boat. His wife had three sons, the eldest eleven years old, the second six years old, and the youngest four years old, all living on the boat. Recently, they had been transporting stones from Anhui to Wuxi, docking at the train station wharf in this county. They were scheduled to unload the stones today and reload them onto trains to transport them to Baogai Mountain in Zhenjiang. Unexpectedly, due to the boat's age and disrepair, the bottom of the hold leaked badly. Yesterday (the 18th) at 10:30 PM, it suddenly sank into the river. At that time, Xu and his wife and children had already gone to bed. When they felt water on their bodies, they immediately got up to rescue the children. The youngest son was rescued by his wife, but the eldest and second sons were unable to be saved and drowned in the river, a truly tragic event.

Local Budget Audit Results

The local budget for the 22nd year of the Republic for this county had already been drafted by County Magistrate Yan. This time, Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, convened a meeting of county magistrates from various counties to the province on the 17th of this month to discuss methods for auditing and reducing county budgets. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu of this county was also summoned and went to the province on the 16th to attend. Furthermore, the expenses required for the People's Hospital in this county had also been included by County Magistrate Yan in the local budget for the 22nd year of the Republic, which attracted considerable attention from the province. It has now been decided to officially open on February 1st to benefit the poor.

Jiangyin

Fuzhou Launch Sinks After Collision

In November of last year, Wang Liping and others from Jingjiang organized the Xincheng Shipping Bureau, acquiring a new-style Fuzhou diesel launch. It made daily runs from Xinsheng Port to Luojia Bridge and Baxi Port, carrying passengers for nearly three months. Now, during the winter break for schools, students from various places in Jiangbei purchased through tickets from Nanjing, Shanghai, Wuxi, and Jiangyin to cross the river. On the 17th, the launch carried 26 passengers, including three female students. At about 3:00 PM, while departing from Jiangyin to Xinsheng Port, it passed through the Zhanghuang Port river section and was struck by a black-hulled riverboat coming downstream. The Fuzhou launch sank, and the passengers, drivers, and crew fell into the river. Although rescue efforts were made by various boats, 15 or 16 people drowned. Yesterday (the 18th) at about 2:00 PM, the bureau learned of the incident after the boat failed to arrive. Manager Wang Liping and boat owner Yu Shicheng took a Yihong boat to the scene of the accident to investigate and await the retrieval of the bodies.

Nantong

Standardizing Weights and Measures Throughout the County

The Department of Construction ordered the Nantong County Government to complete the standardization of the new weights and measures system throughout the county by mid-February and specifically scheduled a county-wide general inspection from the 25th to the 28th of this month, confiscating all illegal old instruments.

Jiaxing

Surveying and Mapping Expenses to be Reduced

Jiaxing County is compiling maps, but less than two-fifths of the county has been completed. However, the expenses for the compilers are calculated based on the combination of the visually surveyed mu (unit of land) and the completed mu, with each mu being paid two fen and four li for mapping fees and one fen and two li for book fees. Currently, the visually surveyed mu are easily inflated, leading to excessive expenses. Yesterday, the County Government convened a meeting of various directors to change the calculation method to a per-number basis, regardless of the number of mu in a number, but still paying two fen and four li for mapping fees and one fen and two li for book fees. Furthermore, the tidal land must be reduced by one-fourth. This method will be implemented after it is approved by the Provincial Department. As a result, the salaries given to the compilers in various districts will be suddenly reduced.

Hangzhou

Actively Proceeding with the Construction of the Yuping Railway

It has been decided that the Yuping Railway will first construct the section from Nanchang to Yushan and organize the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Company, which will be fully entrusted to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway by the Ministry of Railways and the Jiangxi Provincial Government. The outline of the company's organization was approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Government meeting on the 15th. Director Ceng of the Department of Construction instructed the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Bureau to start preparations and took advantage of his trip to Beijing to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee to discuss the matter in detail with the Ministry of Railways and other relevant parties. Once he returns to Hangzhou, he can proceed. At the same time, Director Du of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, considering the heavy responsibility of this matter, felt it necessary to personally plan everything and planned to leave the hospital within a week and go to the bureau to make arrangements.

In Niangniangmiaoqian Village near Linpu Town, Fourth District, Xiaoshan, a farmer named Hua Akun, who was quite wealthy, was targeted by bandits. On the 15th at midnight, a large number of bandits broke into the house, first driving the seven members of the Hua family, men and women, into one room and threatening them to remain silent.
