Free Talk

[Commercial Competition] and [Literary Talent]

— Xu Zhimo

Mr. Shen Congwen said: "[Literary talent] combined with [commercial competition] forms our current concept of the term 'Shanghai School'." I think this is incorrect. [Literary talent] and [commercial competition] are actually two things that cannot be [combined]. Historically, literati have always looked down upon merchants, and merchants have always been indifferent to literati, because literati value elegance and consider merchants vulgar, while merchants value practical benefits and consider literati mad. Moreover, literati often rely on the power of officials to exploit merchants, which is most hated by merchants. The two are fundamentally opposed.

Merchants diligently pursue profit, while admiring the lofty pursuits of literati in composing poetry and enjoying the moon. However, there are many people today who compose poetry and enjoy the moon, but they are not necessarily literati, because they may not have the backing of official power. The condition for becoming a literatus is not just [talent], but even more important is official power. So-called literati are actually officials or underlings of officials. When officials are successful, they have no desire nor need to compose poetry and enjoy the moon, but in order to gain a reputation for promoting elegance, they order their underlings to compose and enjoy. These underlings are mostly talented people. However, officials always have times of failure. At these times, they become bored, so they themselves start to compose poetry and enjoy the moon, and become literati. For example, General Wu Ziyu was indeed a hero of his time, but after stepping down from power, he developed a considerable interest in refined pursuits.

In this regard, if there is indeed a distinction between the [Shanghai School] and the [Beijing School] in the literary world, then I believe that [commercial competition] is the characteristic of the former, while [literary talent] is the characteristic of the latter. Shanghai School writers mostly regard manuscript fees as their primary goal, so they cannot avoid unsightly behaviors such as [opportunism] and [weather-vane shifting]. Beijing School writers, on the other hand, are either university professors or hold government positions, living off the resources of bureaucratic institutions. Their foundations are solid, and their salaries are generous, so they do not have to appear as desperate as Shanghai School writers, and therefore do not need to [speculate] or [watch the wind].

Both merchants and literati need money. However, the money used by merchants is directly earned through their own means, while the money used by literati comes in a more roundabout way. It starts from the hands of ordinary people, passes through countless institutions, and when it reaches the hands of literati, the stench has completely disappeared, like eating lamb after being far away from the kitchen. This is where the purity of literati lies. It is also why they can so loudly scold merchants.

But Shanghai is, after all, a complex place. There are indeed as many Shanghai School writers engaged in [commercial competition] as there are carp crossing the river, but there are also some Beijing School writers with [literary talent]. However, the two have never truly [combined], only successfully creating a [Shanghai-Beijing hybrid] circus.

[Appreciating Standard Beauty]

— Cao Juren

Mr. Lin Yutang said: "[The current society is a male society, so people like to paint nude women. In a female society, people would definitely like to draw nude men, and they would definitely call it 'appreciating standard beauty'.]" Then he said: "[A male dog, if it could paint, would definitely consider the thighs of a female dog as the pinnacle of standard beauty. The same goes for a female dog drawing a male dog.]" (My words in Analects, issue 30.) Explaining the root of art from a biological perspective may shock moralists, but philosophers and artists cannot answer this, but here we find a satisfactory answer. Nietzsche said, "[Beauty and ugliness can both be explained in biological terms.]" That is the meaning.

Once the human body reaches puberty, due to the nourishment of internal secretions, several special characteristics appear: the chest suddenly expands, the buttocks develop into curves, the voice becomes very soft, and the hair becomes lustrous; these are all important repositories of beauty. [The close connection between human beauty and secondary sexual characteristics is an undeniable fact. DeGonrmont said: "[If you ask a toad, what is beautiful? It will tell you: its mate is the most beautiful, with two large and round eyes protruding from its small head, a large and flat mouth, a yellow belly, and a cherry-colored back.]" The same principle applies to humans.

But why do Chinese people avoid talking about [human beauty]? Because gentlemen are very sensitive, and the moment sexual organs are mentioned, obscene ideas arise. Mr. Lu Xun said that talented men in the past could write poems of lovesickness just by finding a handkerchief. And Du Liniang in The Peony Pavilion fell in love to death just by dreaming of a man. Under moral vigilance, this kind of love-sick psychology is inevitable; such people certainly dare not face [human beauty] directly. There are also some sex maniacs who see obscene pictures on the streets, obscene porcelain dolls like Jia Baoyu or Lin Daiyu, or practice the so-called [ugly behavior of both sexes], and then think that human beauty is just like this; these people cannot understand [human beauty] either. When it comes to the appreciation of beauty, Chinese people are still far from the standard of health!

Recently, there has been more and more talk about the state of society and people's hearts. In the end, it is nothing more than advocating old morality; all the sins of old morality in damaging human nature and the human body are passed over without mentioning. I believe that only by popularizing biological knowledge, facing the facts head-on, and not distorting the explanations, can the state of society and people's hearts gradually turn for the better. Darwin wrote in The Descent of Man: "[As far as we can judge, the appreciation of beauty shown by most animals is limited to attracting the opposite sex.]" And cited the nest-building behavior of a bird called Bower-bird as proof. What makes moralists tongue-tied is plain and unremarkable in biology and requires no surprise.

Some people think that Mr. Lin Yutang is deliberately making strange arguments, so I extend his meaning to clarify it as above.

Sickness

— Li Huiying

My wife is sick.

She lies in bed all day and all night, as if the god of sleep has taken away her soul. Even if she slept for a whole year, she wouldn't say she slept too much. Only mealtime is the only time she leaves the bedside. As a result, the small room seems much colder and deathly silent, so stuffy that you can't even take a long breath. Some scattered objects are covered in a layer of dust, and some simply seem to be sulking because they haven't been taken care of by their mistress. All this is because of my wife's illness, which has deprived them of someone to take care of them. A man can only sigh at the scattered things, and rarely gets into the habit of carefully tidying them up. My wife's illness is indeed a great torment to her physically, but she rarely groans or cries, probably because she's afraid of making me anxious. Even so, my mental state has undergone considerable changes, so that whatever I do, I'm always floating like a cloud in the sky, unable to settle down. I can't stop to think about what steps to take to deal with each current task, how to do it, and to what extent it should be done. Sometimes, I realize how ridiculous and foolish my approach to a certain event was after the fact, and I'm really worried about my abnormal state.

My wife is sick, and I'm almost sick too.

But I'm still a little stronger than her. At least I don't sleep like her! And I can cook for her, open the window for her, let the outside air into the room, let the sun shine on her bed; I can also say some comforting words to her as much as possible.

I'm not sick, I'm a good person.

[Why did the illness fall on me?]

Sometimes, just as she finished her meal and before lying down on the bed, my wife would say this to herself. She was anxious.

Hearing her words, I didn't know how to answer at that time. Really, how can people like us, who have difficulty eating even a mouthful of rice, still afford to get sick? Only rich people can afford to be sick for a long time. If people like us are sick, I'm afraid some big doctors will have no food to eat. We can't afford to see a doctor. We don't have that much spare money. The illness grows on our bodies, and we can only let it take its course. But I have to put my wife at ease, so I can only pretend to smile and say to her:

[Don't worry, you'll be better in a few days.]

As soon as I said this, I felt a little embarrassed again. A husband who can't take out money for his wife to see a doctor should just leave his wife and save her from being so tired.

I can't say whether this idea is correct, because there are still some people who advocate that a wife doesn't have to rely on her husband to maintain her life.

I don't therefore admit that poor people shouldn't have wives. On the contrary, a man should have a wife, and a woman should have a husband. Poverty, wealth, and illness are another matter.

My wife is sick, and I'm sick too. We don't know when we'll get better. My wife said, [Why did the illness fall on me?] I want to ask further:

[Why can't we see a doctor?]

Half a Day in Songjiang (Continued)

— Hua Shangwen

He bought a pack of cigarettes, took one out, and put it to the goat's mouth. It sniffed it with its nose, then swallowed it into its mouth and chewed it like grass. Someone gave it a lit cigarette, but it avoided it.

Mr. C said again: [So it's strange, it doesn't eat lit cigarettes.]

But when Mr. C himself gave it a lit cigarette and an unlit cigarette mixed together, it chewed it without hesitation. We were worried and waited beside it for a while, but it showed no signs of pain. Presumably, its mouth wasn't burned. At that time, a friend laughed and said that Mr. Lin Yutang used to praise beggars who smoked opium. If he saw this goat, he would probably write a long article to praise it. Not far from the Dongyue Temple is the Xilin Temple, our destination. The pagoda is called the Xilin Pagoda, standing in front of the main hall. When the monk saw a large group of tourists coming in, he took out the key and came out, reaching out for money to open the door. After some discussion, the door at the bottom of the pagoda was opened, but no one wanted to go up. I thought that maybe I could see Taihu Lake from above, so I volunteered to be the first to run up. Several people followed. The stairs were very narrow, but not very high. When I reached the top floor, I did see a few pieces of vast water in the distance. I felt that it didn't look like Taihu Lake, so Mr. S, who was acting as a guide, told me: [That's not Taihu Lake, that's Mao, which is the three Maos mentioned in the books.] I couldn't help but feel a little disappointed. I could also see a pagoda in the distance. According to Mr. S, that was the Fangta Pagoda, because the pagoda is square. So, this pagoda should be called the Octagonal Pagoda. I think the name Fangta Pagoda is probably a common name. Unfortunately, it was already late, and the Fangta Pagoda was far away, so we didn't go.

In the dim twilight, we walked back the way we came. We crossed a small bridge, turned right, and arrived at the Shanghai-Songjiang highway. At this time, no cars had passed by, and the empty ground seemed even more desolate. It is said that the buses stop running after four o'clock, fearing danger. After leaving the highway, we walked into an alley. After walking not far, Mr. S stopped in front of a bungalow and said:

[Inside is the Wall Tomb. Would everyone like to see it?]

There was no answer, but everyone followed him in. In the middle of the courtyard stood a short Western-style tombstone, with some horizontal sentences engraved on it. At first glance, it looked like celestial script and couldn't be read. Later, I saw the English engraved on the back, and then I realized that it was a direct translation of the English, and the reading order was also from bottom to top. The gentleman who translated these English sentences was very good. If he understood a little philosophical jargon, he might have shown off something like [the symbol of life] [the life of the symbol].

This is just an aside. What made people feel emotional at that time was General Wall himself. Speaking of Wall, people of our generation probably all know him. The stories of the Ever Victorious Army were recorded in the Chinese and history textbooks of elementary schools at that time, and the three names of Wall, Burgevine, and Gordon were deeply imprinted in our immature minds. After the Xinhai Revolution, the high tide of the revolution swept away the stale ideas in our minds. The Taiping Heavenly Kingdom became the precursor of the revolution, and the three great idols of Zeng, Zuo, and Li, who were famous for a generation, were denounced as national traitors and collaborators. People like Wall were naturally snubbed, but no one had recognized their true colors. Some people may not admit that Zeng and Li's creation of the Ever Victorious Army was to use the power of foreigners to slaughter Chinese peasants for the Manchu Qing, while others said that the [Longhairs] also had a foreign background. This is nothing more than mutual slander. Now, everyone understands. Wall and the other two were neither meritorious officials of the Manchu Qing nor good friends of Zeng and Li. They were really the executioners of the first suppression of the Chinese revolution by imperialism. The Manchu Qing was too weak! Therefore, international imperialism helped him organize the Ever Victorious Army. What is amazing is that the nationalities of Wall (American), Burgevine (French), and Gordon (British) were completely different, but they were consistently involved in training the Ever Victorious Army to slaughter Chinese peasants. This reminds people of how Yuan Shikai used advisors from various countries, and the result was that they all unanimously advised him to advance to the throne. This is by no means accidental. Moreover, Wall's tombstone was erected by the American Veterans Wall Corps. The fact that American veterans have a Wall Corps reminds people of the Japanese Black Dragon Society of retired soldiers. Thinking about it again and again, I don't understand why foreigners have always been so concerned about China's bandits. Therefore, Wall's monument cannot be easily forgotten.

In the dim twilight, on the train back to Shanghai, I was always thinking about this matter.

Father and Daughter

— Jin Yi

She has recently clearly seen what her father is suffering from again, which makes her feel surprised. Because for a year, her father has been living so well. Although her father's heart was almost in pain every day before; but a year ago, she herself said that she was willing to accompany her father for the rest of her life. At that time, when she saw his eyes containing glistening tears, didn't she also fall into her father's arms and cry bitterly? She wasn't sad, she was recalling how she had known since she understood things that her father had been living lonely, raising her day by day. Although he didn't say it explicitly, she also knew that her father was so afraid that she would fall in love with someone, follow that person, and leave him alone to spend his lonely twilight years; but she told her father that her daughter had the wish to stay by her father's side. She remembered that he had been happy since then, and he seemed younger; but in recent days, she saw that he had become depressed again.

Sometimes she would come in from outside. Her father was already gone, but his cane was still in the corner. When she called the servant to inquire, she only said that he had gone out alone and didn't know where he was. So she picked up the cane and went to look for him according to her own intention. She easily saw him standing alone in a park half a mile away from home, as if he was thinking about something. He would slowly move his steps and walk into the deep forest. She immediately shouted:

[Dad, can you wait for me?]

At this time, he would show a little surprise, stop, turn around, and smile at her with a little joy and a little annoyance on his face.

[You forgot to take your cane, I brought it to you.]

She walked to her father's side, standing on his left, but put the cane in her father's right hand.

Her father looked at her, his eyes flashing with a little light, as if saying: [Why did you come? Can't you let me be alone here?]

She knew that she didn't dare to look at her father's face. She just said it was getting late and led her father back home.

[Are you still afraid of the dark like a child?]

[That's right, Dad, I can't leave you. When it gets dark, I'm afraid you'll abandon me.]

Following her father's words, she deliberately pretended to be a child. She spoke like a child and wrapped her hands around her father's left arm; but her heart was suddenly occupied by sourness, and tears almost dripped from her eyes.

[Dinner is ready, I roasted a chicken for you, and made some soup with water shield bought from Hangzhou, and I also bought you some smoked fish.]

She deliberately babbled.

Editor's Note

In a China where the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted, to promote radio so that it is widespread among the masses, we can only study crystal sets, because crystal sets are cheap to buy, the adjustment procedure is simple, and once a set is purchased, no further expenses are required. Therefore, Japan in the East is even advocating nationwide crystal sets in order to save people's economy, and our China cannot manufacture vacuum tubes by ourselves, so it is naturally more necessary to promote them.

Although crystal sets are simple, there are still many places to study, such as the oscillation of crystals, special crystal set circuits, etc., which all require us to examine. We hope that radio researchers across the country can pay attention to this economical crystal set and study it, and at the same time, we hope that those who promote radio can also pay attention to the economic capacity of the people across the country and promote the nationwide crystal set, which is what we send.

Research on Crystal Sets and Their Reception Distance

— Yi Zhi

Speaking of ordinary crystal sets, people often suffer from unsatisfactory results. What is the reason? In order to improve the efficiency of crystal sets, to be able to receive sound loudly, select sensitively, and receive from a distance, the following four items should be noted, which are briefly described below.

(1) Antenna Circuit

All the electrical energy of a crystal set comes from the oscillation on the antenna. The strength of the oscillation current affects the height of the reception efficiency. Within a certain limit, the selectivity and sensitivity of the antenna have a certain relationship. A short antenna has better selectivity; a high antenna has stronger sensitivity. Often, a short and high antenna is better than a long and low antenna. Therefore, a legal antenna installation can increase the reception efficiency. The following points should be noted during installation: ㈠ The antenna insulator must be good ㈡ The antenna wire must not be too thin ㈢ The antenna height must be above two meters ㈣ The antenna and lead-in wire must not be too long, and the place where it enters the house must be insulated and isolated from other objects ㈤ The wire must be buried in the ㈥ The antenna lead-in wire is too long, solid.

(2) Spectrum

From the antenna, the energy is gathered on the induction and capacitor devices. Changing the size of the , investigate the wavelength and the external same. The harmonic generates vibration. After calling the detector, the stethoscope emits. The path occupies an important part of the crystal set, so attention should be paid to matching. When the induction in the resonant path is made, the diameter should not be too small, and the wire should not be too thin. If the number of turns is increased by observation and wound on a small , the loss of electricity is very large. The selection of capacitors must also be the fixed piece. The insulator of the piece must be good glue. If you choose cardboard, it will easily lose electrical energy in wet weather and moldy rainy seasons, reducing the reception.

(3) Crystal

The crystal completes the detection of the high-frequency current into the audio frequency. The efficiency of its detection is often different on the crystal, so you must adjust the contact to the most important point when using it, then the reception is loud and far away. The quality of the crystal can be distinguished in terms of form and substance. Generally, the surface is more bumpy and radiant, and those with more receiving points are good products. Those with flat and dull surfaces and fewer receiving points are inferior products. The crystal often becomes low in reception due to long-term use. One reason is that dust enters, and the other is that it generates electricity with the air. The method to prevent this is to make the crystal in a glass cover. Also pay attention. Do not touch the crystal with your hands. If there is dust, wipe it with alcohol or scrape it lightly with a knife.

(4) Stethoscope

The quality of the stethoscope depends on its magnetism and the number of turns of the wire. The one used on the crystal set has a minimum resistance of two thousand ohms, which is sensitive to sound. The following conditions must be observed when using the stethoscope: ㈠ Do not knock or subject it to violent vibrations, ㈡ The moisture on the thin wax must be wiped dry from time to time.

Finally, I want to talk about the reception ability of crystal sets. Ordinary crystal sets can receive from about fifty or sixty miles away from a power station of one hundred watts. If it can be researched and improved and used properly, it can reach as far as one or two hundred miles. As for receiving long-wave telegrams, it can be as far as one or two thousand miles. Now that the Central Radio Station has been completed, within a radius of four or five hundred miles, such as Yangzhou, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Qingpu, Wuhu and other places, according to the local radio reports, the Central Radio Station can be received very clearly with a crystal set. It is also said that someone in Hangzhou has received the Central Radio Station with a crystal set, and its reception distance is quite amazing. Therefore, if the crystal set can be used properly, its performance can be better than a single-tube vacuum tube machine with poor circuit. So I hope people don't dislike it for being old and abandon it. Let's all get up and study and improve it together! (The End)

Operating Principle of Crystal Detector

— Cai Guanghua

Before talking about the operating principle of the crystal detector, we should first understand a strange phenomenon. We know that when two different crystals or a crystal and a metal needle touch together, a resistance occurs. This resistance is enough to make the current flowing between the crystals or between the crystal and the metal needle only flow in one direction. This is the single transmission (UnilateratCondcuctivity) of the crystal detector that is commonly spoken of. Such contact has the function of rectification, so it is also called a contact rectifier (Contat·Rectifer)

Suppose we connect an alternating voltage and a contact rectifier together (see Figure 1, AB two crystals in contact), and we use the Y curve in the second figure to represent the original wave, then the rectified wave can be represented by the Y line in the second figure. From the highest and lowest points (Maxima and Minime) of these two curves, we can get a conclusion, that is, although the positive and negative half-wave amplitudes of the original wave are equal (A1 equals A2 Figure 2X), the result of rectification is A1 greater than A2Y (Figure 2), the positive half-wave is greater than the negative half-wave (rectification must be incomplete). The reason is that it is easier for electrons to flow from B to A than from A to B (Figure 1), in other words, two different crystals or a crystal and a metal needle in contact with each other have a rectifying effect. The crystal detector is the pioneer in managing this effect.

In the detection circuit, after the antenna absorbs external radio waves, a radio frequency current occurs in the antenna. A high-frequency voltage occurs at the two ends of the coil. When the current passes through the crystal, according to the above-mentioned contact rectifier function, only the half-wave current flows through the stethoscope. Then, the stethoscope vibrator is caused to perform various different actions into audio waves by the strength of the current.

Because the crystal detector can only receive damped wave radio messages or radio telephones, but cannot receive continuous wave radio messages, so the crystal radio cannot listen to telegrams, which is the biggest shortcoming of the crystal detector.

Special Galena Radio Circuit

— Li Yuanqing

丨Introduction to Two Full-Wave Galena Radios丨

We know that galena can detect signals because it is a unidirectional conductor. Therefore, the audio signal received by an ordinary galena radio is only half the power of the external radio wave, and the other half of the electrical energy has to be discarded. Now, by using two galena crystals placed in opposite directions, the power of the external radio wave can be completely captured. Since the electrical energy received by the radio has doubled, the output volume will naturally increase accordingly.

The first method is to modify the commonly used headphones into two sections, each with two terminals that are not connected to each other (see Figure 3). After connecting according to the circuit in Figure 1, a double power audio signal can be obtained.

Figure 2: The headphones are not modified. First, input the audio signal into the primary coil of two low-frequency transformers, and connect the headphones to the two secondary coils to achieve the same result.

This article aims to save space, so the description is as simple as possible. As for the detailed theory, I will describe it later.

Free Talk

Talking Words

Children's Year and Family Education

— Meng Ruo

Chinese children have always been little valued by people. Fortunately, they have been brought out by society to hold a [Children's Year]. [Children's Day] has been stipulated in almost all modern civilized countries long ago. European and American countries, and even Japan, pay close attention to children's affairs. The establishment of children's parks, children's libraries, nurseries, children's training homes, and juvenile delinquent reformatories has become commonplace. Only our backward China has not seen anyone organize children's affairs, and the status of children has not been clearly recognized. How can we know that children are the lifeblood of society, country, and nation; their relationship to the civilization of society, the survival of the country, and the rise and fall of the nation is of utmost importance. Therefore, if we want to transform society, transform the country, and transform the nation, we should start with children first. This is the meaning of holding this year's [Children's Year].

The expectations of [Children's Year] for children, generally speaking, are nothing more than to enable every Chinese child to become a physically and mentally healthy citizen in the future, so as to seek welfare for the future of society, country, and nation. The strength of personal physical and mental health is half due to innate heredity and half due to acquired cultivation. Leaving aside the innate heredity for the moment; the tool for acquired cultivation is of course education; and education is divided into family education and school education, the former being more important than the latter, so let's just talk about this aspect.

The status of children in Chinese families is very low; they are often regarded as private property by their parents. Parents in ordinary families either regard children as a [comfort item], or as a [tool for preventing old age], or [inheritors of ancestors' incense], they have almost no awareness that children bear a major mission, that they are the backbone of the future society, the beams of the country, and the pioneers of the nation. Therefore, the parents' concept of their children is wrong: therefore, they do not pay attention to the family education of their children. Parents in general wealthy families treat their children with a completely laissez-faire attitude; they only know how to indulge them and give them full satisfaction in enjoyment, while forgetting the obligations they should fulfill in education. As a result, many children who have no ability, lack knowledge, are arrogant and lazy are cultivated, leaving endless disasters for the future society and country. As for the majority of poor families, the parents are driven by life and work like cattle and horses, they are too busy running around for food and clothing, where do they have the time to educate their children? Moreover, some have never received education and training themselves, and do not even know what family education is. And their children, because they live in hunger and cold, not only do not get beneficial education in spirit; they also often feel a lack of material nutrition, which affects their physical development. The result of this type of family is also nothing more than creating a large number of unhealthy members for society and the country, which is also unfavorable to the community. This is the main reason for the formation of the current corrupt Chinese society. Therefore, to save the ills of Chinese society, we must first raise the status of children; and to raise the status of children, we must start with the implementation of family education. Otherwise, no matter how loud the social figures shout [Children's Year]! [Children are the future masters of the country]! it is just empty talk and does not help the reality.

Regarding the points to be noted in the implementation of family education, there are several important points: 1. Cultivate good habits in children; 2. Improve the bad environment of children; 3. Pay attention to children's diet, daily life, and hygiene; 4. Forge children's strong physique; 5. Nurture children's beautiful character; 6. Instill children's patriotic beliefs; 7. Promote children's desire for knowledge; 8. Guide children's self-government ability; 9. Cultivate children's resolute will, 10. Train children's labor spirit; 11. Promote children's group thinking; 12. Pour children's social awareness; 13. Instruct children's correct behavior, and so on. As for the implementation method, the most appropriate steps can be selected according to the family situation, social needs, and children's interests, and they can be taught, educated, induced, and guided step by step. On the one hand, they should also be sent to school to receive more knowledge and improve their cultivation, so that children can become physically and mentally healthy citizens, and benefit the future society, country, and nation, then the community will benefit a lot! May the parents of our country's families never give up this important responsibility of educating children, this is what we hope for!

Dying Embers

— Mi Er

It is very unlucky to talk about [death] at the beginning of this new year. This is the custom. In fact, this kind of custom is entirely psychological, and how does it conform to the facts? For example, according to the old custom, when we meet in the New Year, we must say [Congratulations and get rich!] This old-fashioned greeting is naturally an auspicious word, and it has been said dozens of times, but he will never get rich because of it! Besides, [death] is unavoidable for everyone. What's the harm in talking about it?

However, this word [death] is fundamentally a terrible word. Dr. Johnson, a great British writer of the eighteenth century, was erudite and talented, and was almost the mainstay of the literary and artistic circles of the time. He had great courage to fight against the harsh environment, but when he heard [death], he would involuntarily tremble and be horrified! The terror of [death] is self-evident. However, no matter what, we will eventually avoid the invitation of [death]!

Christianity tells us that we live in the world just like travelers. It means that we will eventually [return to our old home]. Indeed, we have never heard of a person who does not die. However, we are all alive, and of course we do not know the suffering of death. However, we believe that except for a few exceptions, most people cannot help but regret their sins before they die. Newspapers often report that before the execution of bandits, they often advise the audience not to learn from them, and must be good people. Isn't this an expression of his repentance? According to common sense, people are usually ill before they die. This period of illness is probably the moment when people repent or make happy memories before they die, right? Some people are keen on public welfare or benevolent and generous throughout their lives. When they are about to die, they recall all the good deeds in their lives and feel endless joy. People like this can use their natural energy to bear the responsibilities that human beings should bear, and therefore all the joy is the supreme joy of life. But some people, like Zheng Xiaoxu, who stole the country, or politicians, bureaucrats, and villains who trapped the people in misery, unless they die of a sudden illness, what they want to say at the time of death is probably a word of repentance, right? But what can that repentance do for the facts at that time? Some military and political figures repent of their past military sins by saying scriptures and worshiping Buddha. However, their repentance is mostly after being disappointed and out of office, not when they are in power and have great achievements, so their repentance has nothing to do with our ordinary people. In other words, their repentance after doing evil cannot alleviate the pain of us being trapped in misery. In short, death is unavoidable for everyone. If you want to get supreme joy in the short process of life, a person must at least achieve the most perfect results within the possible scope in his position. A student who cannot study hard at ordinary times, and plagiarizes without cheating during the exam, a merchant who operates prohibited goods, a teacher who misleads students, a soldier who cannot defend the country, a politician who cannot benefit the country... No matter how comfortable the lives of such people are, their conscience will be as painful as if ten thousand arrows are shot at them at the moment of death!

Is this completely out of our ideal? No, the confession of the criminals who are about to be executed is our best example!

Do we want to get supreme happiness? Then please do our part first and resolve to be a people who benefit society.

The Abandoned Child

Our alley is equipped with a trash can in the first house of each alley. Besides the garbage next to the trash can, what we often find are abandoned children. Today, another one was found. Mom told me [Today there is a child wrapped in yellow cloth next to the trash can, probably only eight or nine days old, with a pair of black and shiny little eyes, looking around lively and lovely, inside the wrapping cloth are the child's birth date and ten yuan, this is for the person who takes in the child. This must be the daughter of someone's family, who conceived an illegitimate child and had no way to abandon it after giving birth.] Then Mom said again: [This child is a boy! And he is very cute, I really want to bring him in and make him your sister-in-law's son, you see, your sister-in-law has been in my house for ten years, and it goes without saying for me and your brother, even our relatives and friends are so eagerly looking forward to it, and they are all waiting anxiously, and gradually feel disappointed. I don't know why your sister-in-law makes vows to recite Buddha, kowtows and worships, and eats some fairy prescriptions and magic medicines, but she doesn't see any effect, and she doesn't give birth to a son or raise a daughter. Because of this, the family is out of harmony, and the economy is overflowing. Your brother takes a concubine outside, and your sister-in-law is sick and takes medicine at home... Today this child is very good, and he is a boy, but my family does not allow a foster son to enter the genealogy and inherit the ancestors, so the rice and food are still nowhere to be found, and finally, if the 'adopted son' dies, he is not allowed to enter the hall, so after thinking about it, I still can't figure out a reason.] After Mom said this, she walked away because of something, leaving me alone in the room. Ah! I thought, how contradictory are the things in society! In my mind, I imagined the situation of the abandoned child's mother, she 丨丨the child's mother, now the pain she is suffering in her heart is so heavy! Anyone loves her own biological children, and of course she is no exception. She wraps ten yuan around the child and puts the child's birth date away. When she gets the child ready to throw away, how shattered should her heart be! She must be suffering from other people's rumors and discussions, and the family's ridicule and scolding... This is because she should not have given birth to this child; my sister-in-law, she desperately wants a child, but she doesn't have one, so my brother has changed his mind, and Mom, who is eager to have a grandson, is also very unhappy. No matter how my sister-in-law can't work hard for this, the family has become out of harmony... This is also because she is asked to have a child but she doesn't have one. Isn't this ridiculously contradictory? Having a child but not having the child's father (the so-called official father), society has no one to attack, not having a child also has to suffer the same similar pain, isn't this the height of farting?...

Page 21

[Spiritual Civilization] and [Assimilation]

— He Juefu

I spent a few months with several compatriots who were born in foreign countries. Silently observing their gentle temperament and elegant demeanor, I was reminded of another thing.

I remember when I was studying in elementary school, among my dozens of little companions, there were several children who were born overseas and had never been educated and influenced by the ancestral country of [the land of propriety and righteousness]. Their skin, hair, speech, and actions were no different from ours; but their temperament, temper, and attitude towards things were particularly different.

Because we are children, we don't do things very seriously and reasonably, this is a fact, but we don't do everything and immediately start fighting when we encounter something unfavorable to us. In our eyes, almost anything that is considered likely to cause danger or increase difficulty. Even if we know that we are being wronged, we mostly endure and retreat. However, these children who were born in foreign countries do not completely agree with us. No matter what you are doing or saying, as long as it offends them, no matter how much strength the other party has, they will eventually give you a good revenge before they can feel at ease and calm down. In the meantime, although they have also suffered many embarrassing counterattacks, their tough temperament and irritable temper have never been easily changed.

At that time, my age was very young, and of course I couldn't resist them in terms of strength, but being classmates with them and arguing and quarreling was unavoidable; therefore, after studying in elementary school for a few years, I don't know how many times I suffered from them. I still remember that every time I was wronged, I always ran to my mother with pain and tears to complain. After listening to my words, she often put on an angry face, half comforting me and half scolding them, saying:

[They are bastards, they are barbarians! Don't play with this group of people who don't understand etiquette in the future!]

[Barbarian], what a vicious term! Because I have suffered from their anger many times, the vicious term [barbarian] is firmly in my mind like the ugly face of a demon. After entering middle school, the bad impression that [barbarian] gave me has not faded at all, and there are indeed many [barbarians] among my classmates; however, there are not many who are as unreasonable as those in elementary school. Therefore, after spending a few years in middle school, I reluctantly got along with a few slightly satisfactory [barbarian] friends.

Now, I have been in college for a long time, here, if it weren't for the fact that time has passed for a long time, and I have gleaned some news from chatting with my classmates, and I wanted to identify those who are irritable and strong [barbarians] from their temperament and personality, it would be impossible; except for these few that I am familiar with, their temperament is just as kind, gentle, and honest as those of us who were born in the right way,... Silently thinking about these things, I deeply realized the greatness of the so-called [spiritual civilization] and [assimilation] that our compatriots often pride themselves on.

[Society Is School]

— Liao Zhi

The slogan [Society is School] has been promoted for a while in Europe and the United States, and has been realized, but in our country, there has not been much response. Originally, people are social animals and cannot live apart from society, and schools are a kind of group in society, and they cannot be independent of the circle of society. And the facts tell us that people's lives are progressing day by day. Relying solely on narrow school education to cope with the complex living environment is simply impossible. Therefore, caring educators see this shortcoming, know that simple school education is no longer sufficient to meet the needs of society, and expand the scope of schools, advocating [Society is School] to conform to the trend of this new era. Their original intention is to tear down the walls of the school and tell students to broaden their horizons and go to society to experience the practical life in various aspects, so that they can leave the school and join social groups to engage in activities in the future. From a practical and theoretical point of view, this should be regarded as a new education theory that is extremely in line with the times and worthy of our encouragement.

Our country's education is on the verge of bankruptcy, which is not an exaggeration. Although the major universities and middle and primary schools across the country have worked hard to produce batches of graduates every year, this is a considerable amount in terms of quantity, but in practice, these students who can be said to have completed their studies, once they leave the school and run into society, not only is what they have learned not used, but even the extremely simple social environment cannot be coped with. What is the reason for this? This is because our country's education has always separated schools and society too far. Their schools are their schools, and society is its society, and schools and society have become almost unrelated. Therefore, students are far away from social life, and they work hard in schools for several years. The knowledge and skills they get in the end, once they are moved into society for application, they will run into walls everywhere! The reason why there is such a lack of various talents in our society today, and the reason why a group of graduates have no way out, is nothing more than the result of this reason. This is the result that Chinese education has shown us today!

Therefore, for the sake of our country's education future, the current urgent task should first be to remove this layer of separation between schools and society, and integrate schools and society into one. Schools and society must be closely related. Schools must always pay attention to the changing situation of society, and society should provide schools with assistance in various ways, so that students can personally enter society to experience and acquire various practical knowledge in social life. Only in this way can we relieve one of the ills of Chinese education today.

Modern Celebrities' Paintings and Calligraphy

— Zhou Run, style name Jingren, from Nanhui

Page 23

Suggestions for Our Middle School Readers

We, the editors, are not very satisfied with today's middle school students because their lives still have many shortcomings. For example, male middle school students tend to be lazy, romantic, melancholic, have confused thoughts, and behave eccentrically. Female middle school students are often extravagant, don't study hard, and focus on appearance. These are all things we need to examine and rectify. Especially for the young students who have just entered middle school, you should be particularly strict with yourselves. Now, I will write down a few points that middle school students should pay attention to.

Grasp Your Environment and Understand the Purpose of Studying. Mechanical materialists have already shown us that the environment can control human beings. At the same time, dialectical materialism tells us that human beings can also transform the environment. The objective environment can determine our lives, so we should plant the seeds of creation, so that new environments can emerge from the old ones. Middle school students should pay attention to this point. In addition, what is the purpose of studying? I can answer simply: [Learning for application]. We must apply our knowledge to practical life, then we will not fail the mission of learning. The so-called [He who excels in study can follow an official career] is truly absurd.

Make Life Disciplined. A romantic life is most harmful to both body and spirit. Playing when you should be working, and working when you should be playing is a common problem. This should be changed. Live an absolutely disciplined life, that is, study hard when you are studying, and play hard when you are playing. This will not only benefit your physical health, but also greatly improve your study efficiency.

Develop a Strong Physique. The new explanation of the word "[genius]" is "[constant effort]". Effort requires a strong physique as its foundation. "[A sound mind in a sound body]" is such a wise saying. Mr. Cai Yuanpei once urged us to "[develop a physique like a lion]". If we want to study advanced knowledge, we need constant effort. To be able to make constant effort, we need a strong physique. How to develop it? By focusing on exercise.

Avoid Contact with the Opposite Sex. Most middle school students are between the ages of twelve and eighteen, which is the period of the most drastic physiological development and psychological changes. Reason is not yet fully developed, but emotions are very intense. There is a strong desire for the opposite sex. Therefore, if you occasionally come into contact with the opposite sex, you may inevitably fall in love and pursue them regardless of everything. As a result, you will inevitably make a mess of things, and you will completely forget about studying, and only know how to be with your lover every day.

Be Persistent and Humble. [Haste makes waste]. Learning is difficult to achieve quickly. So, what should we do? In my opinion, academic success comes from [accumulation], and the foundation of accumulation is persistence. If you are happy today, you will work hard and forget to eat, holding the book and reading it desperately. Once the interest is gone, you will put it on the shelf and ignore it for days. Such [spurts of diligence followed by long periods of laziness] will never be effective. Secondly, humility is also very important. Some young people, once they have achieved something, immediately boast about themselves, which is truly a fatal blow to their studies. We must not forget the wise saying [Pride invites loss, humility brings benefit].

Study More on Your Own Outside of Class. To be honest, as for school education, if you want to get abundant knowledge in the classroom, that is impossible. In the classroom, you can only get some knowledge of the doorway and tools. In other words, teachers can only point us in a direction. The long journey still needs to be walked by ourselves. Mr. Chen Dingmo once said in an article on research methods: [What we learn in school is only an overview of knowledge and methods of seeking knowledge]. This is absolutely right. If you want to enrich your knowledge, you still need to work hard on your own. Moreover, middle school students should pay more attention to one or two relatively specialized subjects, so that even if they cannot continue their studies after graduation, they will have a skill to make a living. This is especially needed in the current chaotic society, because objective facts have clearly shown us this.

Amateur Mailbox

The Problem of Food and Lodging for Employees

Dear Editor:

I am from another place. Through the introduction of relatives, I came to work in the accounting department of a foreign firm in Shanghai. My monthly salary is twenty-two yuan, but it does not include food and lodging. (Lunch is provided, but it is not available on Sundays.)

When I first came to Shanghai, the person who introduced me helped me find food and lodging. He introduced me to stay temporarily at his relative's house, and I paid him seven yuan a month for food and lodging. I slept in the living room, which was set up at night and taken down in the morning. The living room was a thoroughfare, and they also played cards late at night, so I often couldn't sleep well. I had to find another way and consult with relatives and friends. However, the relatives with families did not have much spare room in their houses, and the friends were all clerks who ate other people's food and could not make decisions to let me stay for a long time (one or two months was possible). It was not cost-effective to pay for a meal, and even if I reluctantly paid for a meal, the restaurant was unwilling to deliver it. Therefore, both living and eating were major problems, especially living was the most difficult to solve. Because I couldn't borrow accommodation from others, I had to rent a house myself, but most of the houses in Shanghai [do not ask about families], and it is difficult for single people to rent. Therefore, I had to move my family to live in a cheap rental area. (Attic room in the city is eight yuan). However, my monthly income is only twenty-two yuan, how can I cover the expenses of clothing, food, housing, entertainment, etc.? If my wife goes out to work, there are two young children who cannot be left alone. Therefore, I have to go into debt every year for the sake of my job.

Dear Editor, in my situation, if I don't bring my family, I have no place to eat and live. If I bring my family, I don't have enough to spend and I have to go into debt. Isn't it more painful to have a job! But if I quit my job, how can my family sit and eat at home, plus it's a matter of reputation; if I look for another job, it's even more difficult! Therefore, I have been worried every day since I came to Shanghai because of the problem of food and lodging, and there is no solution. Now I see in the newspaper that

You can solve difficult problems for people, so I specially send a letter with the details, and please provide guidance and answers as soon as possible. I beg you,

Sincerely, Yu Ruisheng

Editor's note: This is a problem that is very easy to solve, and at the same time, it is a problem that has no solution at all. Because if your income is very high, then clothing, food, and housing can all be satisfactory, so how could such a problem arise? Therefore, the center of the problem is not the inability to solve the problem of clothing, food, and housing, but the economic difficulty. The income cannot meet the expenses. According to your monthly income, it is already very difficult to maintain a personal life, let alone support a family. Therefore, your so-called [food and lodging problem] is the entire living problem. The best solution for individuals to this problem is to increase income, but the society is full of unemployment. It is really [easier said than done] to find a job with a higher salary. Therefore, this problem cannot be solved by individual efforts.

Then, should we just wait to die and starve to death? No! No! Absolutely not! We must not succumb to the difficulty of knowing how to live and the harshness of the environment. Instead, we must fight to create a new environment and a new life, and fight to the death!

How do we create a new environment and a new life? Regarding this, we can answer: the difficult situation you are suffering is not just your individual problem, but the pain that everyone who lives on a salary feels. This kind of pain cannot be eliminated by individual efforts alone. Instead, people who share this pain need to unite and study the origins of this pain together, think of ways to relieve this pain, and at the same time work together to implement solutions to this difficulty. Only in this way can your difficulties be resolved; otherwise, we are just like you, with no solution to this problem.

The answer we have given to this letter is just a general direction for solving the problem. As for specific methods, we hope that readers will come up with them for public discussion. The reason why we want to publish this letter is that although this problem is currently impossible to solve in society, it is the most serious problem for ordinary people. Therefore, we hope that people who care about social problems or the future of society will pay close attention to this problem; at the same time, we hope that people who are personally experiencing this difficulty will carefully consider this problem and come up with a solution.

Novel

Man's Evil Freedom (2)

— Man Zhi

I went to your house the next afternoon. This time, you probably thought I was a regular visitor, so you didn't ask me to sit on the cold bench in the living room. You welcomed me into your room. Although I remembered what happened last time, I didn't think much about it and sat down in the room. I like to play Go. I invited you to the round table to play Go. You agreed, but your thin face was like the clear blue sky of autumn, covered with a gray cloud. Although I thought you must have something unhappy on your mind, how could I ask you directly? Although I was playing Go, I wasn't happy; and you were fighting aimlessly, and finally couldn't finish the game and sighed!

You started by saying, [Yesterday, you and Renjie went to see a play and drink alcohol. He also went to the Jai Alai court and lost all his money before coming back. You are his old friend, and you should advise him!]

This was a complaint from the wife to the husband's old friend! I was shocked! You should have seen the surprise in my eyes then, right?

I said, [Yesterday, we went to see [Grand Hotel], and then went to [Jie Er Jing] to eat. He said he went to the Jai Alai court to relax, and I also advised him not to be so decadent.]

You said, [He has been really decadent lately. Since living with me, there hasn't been a day without a quarrel. He's probably decadent because he lives with me. I really don't want to harm him and let him continue to be decadent!]

[He's too ungrateful to me,] you said, tears streaming down your face and your voice choked up. [You probably know that he was with Lu Bixia before, right? He treated Lu Bixia so well, whatever she said was what she got. Her words were like God's commands; how does he treat me? No matter how much I advise him, my words are like wind blowing past his ears! In the past year, all the royalties or school salaries he received were sent to the Jai Alai court. Every time I advise him not to throw money into the sea like that, he doesn't listen at all, as if he's drunk, and has no reason at all. He also likes to drink alcohol, at least three or four bottles at a time, and no matter how much you advise him, you can't bring him back. He often laughs coldly or loudly abnormally after drinking. I asked him if he had any worries or troubles in his heart, but he didn't say anything. He's like a madman. He's obviously worried and troubled in his heart, but he doesn't tell me. How can I know what he's worried about? In this way, I comforted him, but I don't know which words can truly comfort his heart. I'm living a worried and uneasy life. I'm worried and uneasy for him, but I can't show my worries and unease in front of him. How can I live on?

[The mental pain is like this, and he doesn't care about the material things either. Look at the room, which is a mess. He doesn't even pay for sofa covers. The clothes I wear are all old, and the rent is two months overdue. He keeps saying he has a solution, but where will the solution come from? When he was with Lu Bixia, I heard from friends that Lu Bixia had a suit made today and two cheongsams made tomorrow. Let's not talk about that, he doesn't even care about himself, and he needs someone to take care of him. He's really too ungrateful to me!

[Moreover, we often quarrel, and he takes out his anger on me. Am I something to be vented on? …I can't take it anymore!]

You said angrily and sadly. At that time, I found it difficult to say anything. I sympathized with your suffering, but I could also forgive Renjie's willfulness; moreover, what can a third party say about a couple's affairs? If I say you're wrong, you'll definitely be unhappy. If I say he's wrong, you'll scold me in the future, even tomorrow, when you're in love. So, at that time, I sympathized with your suffering, and I didn't speak ill of Renjie. Do you remember? At that time, I just sighed and said,

[Renjie has been deeply stimulated recently, and he's going down the road of decadence!]
